### 3.22.4.5 Slot for the Downlink Control Information of the SIB1 on the PDCCH

**3.22.4.5.0-1**  (ID: `11165075`)

Slot for the Downlink Control Information of the SIB1 on the PDCCH
11165075:
Slot for the Downlink Control Information of the SIB1 on the PDCCH
The slot where the Downlink Control Information (DCI) is broadcasted for a given SIB1 transmission is computed according to the following data:
 SS/PBCH Block index.
 The type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex.
 The frequency range.
 The SIB1 pattern selected for the SI window (see the previous section).
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a blurry, light-colored font on a dark background. The formula appears to be:
slotSib1ss/PBCH = (0 x 2μ + [M x absIndexss/PBCH] + slotOffseti) mod Nslotframe,μ
The formula calculates a value related to "slotSib1" for "ss/PBCH", which likely refers to a synchronization signal/physical broadcast channel in a telecommunications context. The formula involves multiplication, addition, an absolute value, and a modulo operation. The variables used are:
\* `slotSib1ss/PBCH`: The value being calculated.
\* `μ`: A Greek letter, likely representing a subcarrier spacing or numerology.
\* `M`: A variable, possibly a multiplier.
\* `absIndexss/PBCH`: An absolute index related to the ss/PBCH.
\* `slotOffseti`: An offset value.
\* `Nslot`: A value related to the number of slots.
\* `Nframe,μ`: A value related to the number of frames for a given `μ`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11422.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
O and *M:*
Parameters defined according to the type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex and frequency range as follows.

### 3.22.4.6 Slot for the Transport Block (TB) of the SIB1 on the PDSCH

#### 3.22.4.6.0-1 Slot for the Transport Block (TB) of the SIB1 on the PDSCH The PDSCH associated to the grant for a given SIB1 is always sent in the same slot as the PDCCH. (ID: 11165090)

### 3.22.4.7 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1

#### 3.22.4.7.0-1 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 PDCCH resource allocation (ID: 11165100)

**3.22.4.7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11165111`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
According to the type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex, frequency range and the SS/PBCH blocks configured [CB008285-E-UPD001], activated (nActivatedSsPbch) and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], the slot handles one or two DCI Format 1\_0 for two consecutive SS/PBCH blocks. Each DCI is sent in a common search space associated to the SS/PBCH block.

---

#### 3.22.4.7.0-2 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 Time Domain resource allocation (ID: 11165116)

**3.22.4.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12516735`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
The time domain of the common search space is linked to the type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex, the number of OFDM symbol for the Control Resource Set (CORESET) defined through the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex NIDD parameter and frequency range.

The 5G-L2-PS computes the parameter startSymbolNumber for the DlData\_PdcchSendReq message from the following tables.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency Range 1 Starting OFDM Symbol of common search space for the SIB1 transmission |  |  |  |
| type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex | Even SS/PBCH block | Odd SS/PBCH block |  |
| 0 | 0 |  |  |
| 1 | 0 | CORESET(0) duration |  |
| 2 | 0 |  |  |
| 3 | 0 | CORESET(0) duration |  |
| 4 | 0 |  |  |
| 5 | 0 | CORESET(0) duration |  |
| 6 | 0 |  |  |
| 7 | 0 |  | CORESET(0) duration |
| 8 | 0 |  |  |
| 9 | 0 |  |  |

| 12 | 1 |  |  |
| 13 | 2 |  |  |
| 14 | 1 |  |  |
| 15 | 2 |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency Range 2 Starting OFDM Symbol of common search space for the SIB1 transmission |  |  |  |

| 0 | 0 |  |  |
| 1 | 0 | 7 |  |
| 2 | 0 |  |  |

The number of OFDM symbols of the CORESET(0) associated to the common search spaces is defined as follows according to the frequency range, the operating band (specific configuration for n79 [CB009173-B] and n104 [End CB009173-B]), the combinations of the common and SS/PBCH sub-carrier spacings and the value of the NIDD parameter type0CoresetConfigurationIndex.

Note: The type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex must be configured properly to ensure there are enough PDSCH slots for SIB1 transmissions, considering TDD frame structure, SSB, CSI-RS for tracking (TRS) (see [11164136: SIB1 initial transmission and retransmissions pattern](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktdrvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

~~For example (in this requirement, the validation of the SIB1 slots selected is already successful since a while the example should not be here if needed, it can be in SIB1 slot selection or better in the system module),~~

~~In case of 4 SSBs (nActivatedSsPbch = 4 (see 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), and TDD Frame Structure (UL:DL= 2:8, frameStructureType is 'tdLte'), only type0SearchSpaceConfigurationIndex = 5 can be used because:~~

~~• Value 0, 1, 8 are not possible because SIB1 slots are overlapped with slot of SSB#0.~~

~~• Value 2, 3, 6, 7, 9 are not possible because SIB1 slots are overlapped with uplink slots.~~

~~• Value 4 is not possible because SSB#3 overlapped with special slot.~~

#### 3.22.4.7.0-3 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 Frequency domain resource allocation (ID: 11165134)

**3.22.4.7.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12514655`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
The frequency domain of the common search space (size of the CORESET(0) bandwidth) is defined as follows according to the frequency range, the operating band (specific configuration for n79 [CB009173-B] and n104[End CB009173-B]), the combinations of the common and SS/PBCH sub carrier spacings, the value of the NIDD parameter type0CoresetConfigurationIndex, and the NIDD parameters defining the New Radio-Absolute Radio Frequency Channel Number (NR-ARFCN) and Global Synchronization Channel Number (GSCN).

The 5G-L2-PS uses 2 parameters computed by the C-Plane (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2159\_replaced([11308553](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrE9MfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and sent in the DlData\_PdcchSendReq message to define the frequency domain for the PDCCH resource allocation:

 coresetFreqDomain, bitmap defining the relative position of PRB groups allocated to the control resource set for the SIB1 transmissions.The identifier of the CORESET is equal to 0.

 coresetFreqDomainRbShfit indicating the shift to apply in order to have the absolute position of PRBs within the control resource set.

---

#### 3.22.4.7.0-4 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 Control Channel Element start index (ID: 11165142)

**3.22.4.7.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12514663`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
When the number of Control Channel Elements (CCE) allows several positions of the PDCCH candidate for SIB1 PDCCH allocation, the 5G-L2-PS uses alternatively each of them across the SI window according to the CCE distribution between DL and UL schedulers.

The CCE start positions for each Aggregation Level (AL) allowed are defined below according to the combinations of PRB and OFDM symbol associated to the value of type0CoresetConfigurationIndex.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | CCE start positions |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Aggregation Level | AL4 |  |  |  | AL8 |  | AL16 |
|  | PDCCH candidate | 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 0 | 1 | 0 |
| CORESET configuration | {24,1} | 0 | - | - | - | - | - | - |
| {24,2} | 0 | 4 | - | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {24,3} | 0 | 4 | 8 | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {48,1} | 0 | 4 | - | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {48,2} | 0 | 4 | 8 | 12 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {48,3} | 0 | 4 | 12 | 16 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {96,1} | 0 | 4 | 8 | 12 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {96,2} | 0 | 8 | 16 | 24 | 0 | 16 | 0 |  |
| {96,3} | 0 | 12 | 24 | 36 | 0 | 24 | 0 |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| SS/PBCH SCS (kHz) |  | 15 |  | 30 |  | 30 (n79[CB009173-B] and n104 [End CB009173-B] |  | 120 |  | 240 |  |
| Common SCS (kHz) |  | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 60 | 120 | 60 | 120 |
| type0 Coreset Configuration Index | 0 | {24,2} | {24,2} | {48,1} | {24,2} | {48,1} | {24,2} | {48,1} | {24,2} | {96,1} | {48,1} |
| 1 | {24,2} | {24,2} | {48,1} | {24,2} | {48,2} | {24,2} | {48,1} | {24,2} | {96,1} | {48,1} |  |
| 2 | {24,2} | {24,2} | {48,2} | {24,2} | {48,3} | {24,3} | {48,2} | {48,1} | {96,2} | {48,2} |  |
| 3 | {24,3} | {24,2} | {48,2} | {24,2} | {96,1} | {24,3} | {48,2} | {48,2} | {96,2} | {48,2} |  |
| 4 | {24,3} | {24,3} | {48,3} | {24,2} | {96,1} | {48,1} | {48,3} | {24,2} | - | {24,1} |  |
| 5 | {24,3} | {24,3} | {48,3} | {24,3} | {96,2} | {48,1} | {48,3} | {24,2} | - | {24,1} |  |

#### 3.22.4.7.0-5 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 Aggregation Level selection (ID: 11165160)

**3.22.4.7.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12815898`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
The Aggregation selected for the SIB1 transmissions is defined by the operator through the NIDD dciSiAggregationLevel parameter. [Before CB014330-F] It is transmitted to the 5G-L2-PS in the psCell\_CellSetupReq.[End CB014330-F]

---

#### 3.22.4.7.0-6 PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1 Other parameters for the PDCCH SIB1 transmissions (ID: 11165173)

**3.22.4.7.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11165195`)

PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
11165195:
PDCCH resource allocation for the SIB1
The 5G-L2-PS, also, uses for the dlData\_PdcchSendReq message, the following data related to the PDCCH from the ones configured by the C-Plane through the psCell\_CellSetupReq associated to the coresetId equal to 0:

 cceRegMappingType set to interleaved.

 interleaverRows set to 2.

 regBundleSize set to 6.

 precoderGranularity set to regBundleSize.

 nShiftModNumOfRegBundles computed as specified in the requirement 5G\_L2\_10447\_replaced([11178156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 dmrsScramblingSequenceInit and dciScramblingSequenceInit are set to Physical Cell Identifier and corresponds to the PDCCH scrambling identifier ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N₁D" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a light blue and yellow gradient, with a slight rainbow effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11438.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]).

 pdcchDciTransmitPower

[image-1][image\_desc]pdcchDciTransmitPower = -10 × Log(12 × N\_R^DL) + pdcchPowerOffset[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11438.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

### 3.22.4.8 PDSCH resource allocation

#### 3.22.4.8.0-1 PDSCH resource allocation Resource allocation (ID: 11165209)

**3.22.4.8.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11165216`)

PDSCH resource allocation
To define the number of SIB1 transmissions per SS/PBCH block configured [CB008285-E-UPD001], activated (nActivatedSsPbch) and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], the 5G-L2-PS has computed the number of RB (nRbSib1) and the number of OFDM symbols (see section “SIB1 initial transmission and retransmissions pattern”). With those data, the 5G-L2-PS defines the PDSCH allocation in time and frequency domains.

---

#### 3.22.4.8.0-2 PDSCH resource allocation Time domain allocation (ID: 11165223)

**3.22.4.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165232`)

PDSCH resource allocation
11165232:
PDSCH resource allocation
The time domain resource allocation and index are selected from the following table according to the number of OFDM symbol defined to compute the SIB1 transmissions, the position of the DM-RS type A, the number of SIB1 to transmit in the slot, the time domain of common search spaces and the OFDM symbols dedicated to the downlink. When there are 2 SIB1 to transmit, the 5G-L2-PS selects first and randomly the SS/PBCH index between the two consecutive ones (even and odd) for which the first time domain allocation of SIB1 has to be done. The random function is initialized with the Physical Cell Identity of the cell.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for TD resource allocation index selection. The flowchart begins with a starting point labeled "TD resource allocation index selection."
From the start, a process box states "Set unavailable OFDIvI symbol for Gp and Uplink in the." This leads to a decision diamond asking "2 PDCCH for SIB1 in the slot?".
There are two branches from this decision diamond:
**Branch 1 (Yes to "2 PDCCH for SIB1 in the slot?"):**
1. A process box states "Set unvailable the OFDIvIfor the PDCCH associated to the SS/PBCH block."
2. This is followed by a process box stating "Select the first index with the expect ed length and with the lover start OFDIvI symbol allowed."
3. This leads to a terminal shape labeled "Index of PDSCH TD alocation associated to SS/PBCH."
**Branch 2 (No to "2 PDCCH for SIB1 in the slot?"):**
1. A process box states "Set unvailable the OFD Ivifor the PDCCH for two consecutive SS/PBCHblocks."
2. This is followed by a process box stating "Select randomly the SS/PBCH block considered first (even or odd) or select the remaining one for the SFN."
3. This leads to a process box stating "Select the first index with the expect ed length and with the lover start OFDIvI symbol allowed for the SS/PBCHblock selected."
4. This then leads to another decision diamond asking "2 SIB1 in the slot?".
From the second decision diamond ("2 SIB1 in the slot?"):
**Branch 2a (Yes to "2 SIB1 in the slot?"):**
1. A terminal shape is labeled "Index of PDSCH TD allocation associated to SS/PBCH block."
**Branch 2b (No to "2 SIB1 in the slot?"):**
1. A process box states "Set unavailable the OFDIvI symbols used for the first selected SS/PBCH block TD allocation."
2. This is followed by a process box stating "Select the first index with the expect ed length and with the lover start OFDIvI symbol allowed for the second SS/PBCHblock index."
3. This leads to a terminal shape labeled "Indexes of PDSCH TD allocations associated to SS/PBCHblocks."[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11444.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 3.22.4.8.1 Frequency domain allocation

##### 3.22.4.8.1.0-1 Frequency domain allocation Overview (ID: 11165244)

**3.22.4.8.1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12816250`)

Frequency domain allocation
12816250:
Frequency domain allocation
For FR1 TDD/FDD
 If NRCELL.sibStartPrbRandomDisabled is set to TRUE,
 start RB of SIB1 in the slot shall be set to:
 start RB of coreset #0.
 Else,
The starting RB index of each SIB1 (startRbSib1) in a slot is computed randomly as follows. The random function is initialized with the Physical Cell Identity of the cell.
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula enclosed in a large curly brace. The formula consists of three lines.
The first line states an inequality:
$0 \leq \text{startRbSib1} < (\text{CORESET}(0)\text{size} - \sum\_{0}^{\text{nbSib1}-1} \text{nRbSib1})$
The second line defines a variable:
$\text{startRbSib1}*{\text{firstSsPbch}} = \text{startRbSib1}$
The third line defines another variable:
$\text{startRbSib1}*{\text{secondSsPbch}} = \text{startRbSib1} + \text{nRbSib1}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11450.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
If /NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is True and If NRCELL.sibStartPrbRandomDisabled is set to False, randomly selected startRbSib1 shall be adjusted to multiples of minRBReservedForNonSiPaging (/NRBTS/NRCELL/minRBReservedForNonSiPaging)
With
startRbSib1:
Random value in the allowed starting area of PRB index to transmit the SIB1. The value is computed at each time gNB-DU has to transmit one or two SIB1 in a slot.
CORESET(0)size:
Number of RB defined by the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex value.
minRbReservedForNonSiPaging:
        Minimum *number of RBs reserved for other UEs RNTI that could be used to scheduled using DCI 1\_0 format. (NIDD Parameter /NRBTS/NRCELL/minRbReservedForNonSiPaging)*
**Note: *if NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is False, then the parameter minRbReservedForNonSiPaging shall not be referred.***
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, light-colored text on a white background. The text appears to be "n bStb1".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11450.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:
Number of SIB1, the gNB-DU has to transmit in the slot.
[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains text that reads "n RbStb1". The text is blurry and has a slight blue and yellow tint.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11450.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]:
Number of RB for one SIB1 transmisison defined by the Link Adaptation process.
[image-3][image\_desc]startRbSib1\_firstSsPbch,startRbSib1\_secondSsPbch[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11450.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]:
The first start RB index computed is associated to the first SIB1 selected in the time domain allocation when two SIB1 are transmitted in the slot. The second start RB index is used only for the second SIB1 transmission in the slot if there is one. The second start RB is computing for 2 PDCCH in one slot when FDM of 2 SIB1 is allowed in the same slot.
 
When the DCI 1\_0 for the common channel (SIB1, SI , PAGING), rach msg2, rach msg4 are mapped on CORESET 0 but the DCI 1\_0 in CSS mode for transient phase (Type3 PDCCH CSS , see 38.213 §10.1) are mapped on a CORESET#X (with X>0) (and not on CORESET #0, see 5G\_UP\_10874\_replaced([11350654](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubnt5vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and when the start Prb of the CORESET 0 is lower than the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0),
if the highest PRB of SIB1 is lower than the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0), gNB-DU shall increment the startRbSib1 in order that there is no gap between SIB1 and the CORESET#X (with X>0) PRB area, that is the PRB above the highest PRB of SIB1 is the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0). 
When NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true and [Before CB015668-A] NRBTS.actTddCsiRsOpt = true and NRBTS.actTddCsiImRm = true [CB015668-A] actTddCsiRsOpt = true and actTddCsiImRm = true (note: actTddCsirsOpt and actTddCsiImRm are not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) **[End CB015668-A]**, in TDD FR1 in a CSI-IM slot, if a SIB1 is scheduled in this CSI-IM slot, the starting PRB startRbSib1 of the (lower) SIB1 shall be modulo PRB\_GRANULARITY in order to keep the PDSCH sub areas (startPrb and size) multiples of PRB\_GRANULARITY (see 5G\_UP\_11022\_replaced([11350898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubpjFvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then gNB-DU shall increase of decrease the value of startRbSib1 in this way. 
 
If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, due to the scheduling of SIB1(s) channel(s), gNB-DU shall split the current PDSCH sub area which contains the CORESET #0 in two PDSCH sub areas :
 one which contains the SIB1(s) starting with the startRbSib1 if mono BWP or dedicated BWP bottom aligned and the PRBs which are above the SIB1(s) if dedicated BWP bottom aligned.
 one which contains the PRBs which are below the SIB1(s) if mono BWP or dedicated BWP bottom aligned.
The update and initialization of the PDSCH sub areas are described with more details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23452\_replaced([11175855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kumUKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and are done at to-be-scheduled list update step **of the TD scheduler (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4327\_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

---

#### 3.22.4.8.2 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-1 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Demodulated Reference Signal configuration parameters for the SIB1 transmissions (ID: 11165348)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11165364`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
11165364:
Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS sets the following  Demodulated Reference Signal configuration for the SIB1 transmissions:

 The parameter “dmrsScramblingSequenceInt” is equal to the Physical Cell Identifier NIDD parameter “physCellId” under MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL object.

 The parameter “dlDmrsConfigType” is equal to 1.

 The parameter “dlDmrsLen” is equal to 1.

 The parameter “dlDmrsMappingType” is set according to the Time Domain Resource Allocation saved in the active context of SIB1 and the associated SS/PBCH index (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3710\_replaced([11164737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kteS0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The parameter “dlDmrsAddPos” is equal to 2.

 The parameter “dlDmrsTypeAPos” is equal to the NIDD parameter “dmrsTypeAPosition” under “MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL” object and received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq.

 The parameter “numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData” is equal to 2.

 The parameter “nscId” is equal to 0. This parameter is not used for the SIB1 transmissions.

 The parameter “offsetRbDmrs” is equal to Common RB start index of the Type0-PDCCH search space computed, hereafter, with the position of the CORESET(0) within the whole bandwidth. The first MSB bit set to 1 ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "msbPos" in a blurry, light gray font against a white background. The text is horizontally aligned and appears to be part of a larger word or phrase.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11453.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]) in the coresetFreqDomain parameter of the CORESET(0) and the RB shift ([image-1][image\_desc]The image contains text that reads "coresetFreqDomainRblShlfc". The text is blurry and appears to be in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11453.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]) are received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message.

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
`offset[setRbDmr's = 6 × (63 - msbPos) + coresetFreqDomainRbShift`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11453.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

This part belong to PDSCH DMRS for SIB1, should go to L1 Algortithm.

---

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-2 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Phase Tracking Reference Signal configuration (ID: 11165372)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165378`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS does not activate the Phase Tracking Reference Signal (PT-RS) for the SIB1 transmissions and uses the following setting:

 The parameter “dlPtrsFlag” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsTimeDensity” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsFrequencyDensity” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsNumOfPorts” is set to 1.

 The parameter “dlPtrsResElemOffset” is set to 0.

---

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-3 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Frequency and time domains configuration (ID: 11165385)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11165403`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
11165403:
Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS sets the frequency and time domain configuration for the SIB1 transmisisons as follows:

 The parameter “startSymbol” is set to start symbol of the Time Domain Resource Allocation  selected for the SIB1 transmission and defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3703\_replaced([11164172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kteSwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “numOfPdschSymbols” is set to length of the Time Domain Resource Allocation  selected for the SIB1 transmission and defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3703\_replaced([11164172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kteSwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “startPrb” indicates the absolute position of the SIB1 transmission and takes into account the position of the CORESET(0) within the whole bandwidth. The first MSB bit set to 1 ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "msbPos" in a blurry, light blue font against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11457.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]) in the coresetFreqDomain parameter of the CORESET(0) and the RB shift ([image-1][image\_desc]The image contains blurry text that reads "coresetFreqDomainRblShlfc".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11457.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]) are received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message. The starting PRB of the SIB1 transmission(s) is computed in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3748\_replaced([11165244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktgH-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a blurry, light gray font against a white background. The formula is:
`startPrb = 6 × (63 – msbPos) + coreSetFreqDomainRbShift + startRbSib1_ssPbch`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11457.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

 The parameter “numOfPrb” is set to number of RB compute for the SIB1 and saved in the SIB1 context as defined in the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3716\_replaced([11164922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kte50_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) requirement.

 The parameter “rat0Bitmap” is set to 0x0000, as only the resource allocation type 1 is used for the SIB1 transmissions.

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-4 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Modulation and Coded Scheme (ID: 11165410)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11165414`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS applies the following Modulation and Coded Scheme setting:

 The parameter “mcs” as defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3716\_replaced([11164922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kte50_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “mcsTable” is set to “max64QAM”.

 The parameter “modulationOrder” is set to QPSK (2).

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-5 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Layer to antenna port mapping configuration (ID: 11165421)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11165427`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
For the Layer to antenna port mapping configuration, the 5G-L2-PS applies the following setting:

 The parameter “numOfLayers” is set to 1.

 The parameter “antPort” is set to 0x8000.

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-6 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Precoding antenna port to Radio Unit port settings (ID: 11165431)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11165436`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS applies the following setting for the precoding antenna port to Radio Unit port:

 The parameter “pdschBundleSize” is set to 4 (the UE assumes, without any impact, a bundle size set to 2).

 The precoding and spatial mode parameters are set according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3171\_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO, only C4 is supported for subCell type. one x pol beam is used for SIB1 transmission. More detail refer to 5G\_L2\_497\_replaced([11156027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vT_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The precoding and spatial mode parameters are set according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3171\_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO and for ecpri cells,  “spatialMode” “codebookIndex” shall be set in the same way as cpri cells.

---

##### 3.22.4.8.2.0-7 Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions Beamforming management parameters (ID: 11165443)

**3.22.4.8.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11165450`)

Other parameters for the PDSCH SIB1 transmissions
For the eCPRI configuration, the following parameters are defined for beamforming management.

 numCeAxcIndex. The value corresponds to the number of Radio Unit Antenna ports available for the cell (2 or 4).

 ceAxcIndex. The Value corresponds to the indexes of Antenna-Carrier (AxC) containers selected for the PDSCH transmission in the cell between 0 to numCeAxcIndex-1.

 patternId. The value corresponds to the index of the pattern associated to the beam Index of the selected SS/PBCH for the transmission.

For CPRI configuration, the beamforming management is done by sending the DlData\_PatternConfigReq.

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO, only C4 is supported for subCell type. One x pol beam is used for SIB1 transmission. More detail of CPRI cells refer to 5G\_L2\_497\_replaced([11156027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vT_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of pattern ID for both CPRI and eCPRI corresponds to the index of the pattern associated to the beam Index of the selected SS/PBCH for the transmission.

For CPRI configuration, the beamforming management is done by sending the DlData\_PatternConfigReq.

numOfXpolBeams andpatternIdPolList shall be set according to 5G\_L2\_497\_replaced([11156027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vT_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO and for the eCPRI configuration, the parameters in streamConfig structure are common for CPRI and eCPRI. But for eCPRI only the 1st xpol stream shall be used. Note: FDM has no impact to streams of eCPRI and MU MIMO does not work for SIB.

---

### 3.22.4.9 PDSCH payload management for the SIB1 transmission

#### 3.22.4.9.0-1 PDSCH payload management for the SIB1 transmission (ID: 11165460)

**3.22.4.9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11165479`)

PDSCH payload management for the SIB1 transmission
11165479:
PDSCH payload management for the SIB1 transmission
The 5G-L2-PS receives from the C-Plane in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message the ASN1 encoded SIB1 in a Radio Link Control Transparent Mode (RLC-TM) Paquet Data Unit (PDU).

With the Transport Blocks Size defined during the LA process, the 5G-L2-PS builds a Medium Access Control (MAC) transparent PDU with the RCL-TM PDU and adds 0 padding bits if needed to reach the TBS.

[CB012544-B] If PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq contains the offset to hyperSFN-r17, then L2-PS shall set the hyperSFN-r17 with current hyper SFN (H-SFN) value each time the DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message is sent to the L1. [End CB012544-B]

Then, the 5G-L2-PS build the DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message, in order to send it with the DlData\_PdschSendReq to the L1, with the following parameters:

 The parameter “tbIndex” is set to 0.

 The parameter “tbFragmentOffset\_bits” is set to 0.

 The parameter “tbFragmentSize\_bytes” is computed from the Transport Block Size (TBS) defined during the link adaptation process defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3716\_replaced([11164922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kte50_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light blue font against a white background. The equation is:
$tbFragmentSize\_{bytes} = \frac{TBS}{8}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11469.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

 The payload corresponding to the MAC PDU above.

---

### 3.22.4.10 DCI Format 1_0 content

**3.22.4.10.0-1**  (ID: `11165497`)

DCI Format 1\_0 content
11165497:
DCI Format 1\_0 content
The DCI Format 1\_0 for the SIB1 transmissions is detailed hereafter.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DCI Format 1\_0 size for SI transmissions |  |  |  |
| Field description | Initial BWP size (RB) |  |  |
| 24 | 48 | 96 |  |
| Frequency Domain Resource Allocation | 9 | 11 | 13 |
| Time Domain Resource Allocation | 4 |  |  |
| VRB-to-PRB mapping | 1 |  |  |
| Modulation and coding scheme | 5 |  |  |
| Redundancy version | 2 |  |  |
| System information indicator | 1 |  |  |
| Reserved bits | 15 |  |  |
| Total (without 24 CRC bits) | 37 | 39 | 41 |

The frequency domain resource allocation size is defined according to the value of type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter. The resource allocation type 1 is used. The Resource Indication Value (RIV) is computed with the following information:

 Number of RB for the SIB1 transmission (nRbSib1).

 Number of RB for the CORESET(0) ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N RB CORESET(0)". The text is in a light blue color and appears to be slightly blurred. The "N" is large and in the foreground, with "RB" as a superscript above and to the right of the "N". Below the "N" and slightly to the right is the word "CORESET", and to the right of that is "(0)" in parentheses.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11471.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]).

 Index of the RB start (startRbSib1).

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation defining a piecewise function named `rivSib1`.
The equation is as follows:
$$
rivSib1 = \begin{cases}
N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB} \times (nRbSib1 - 1) + startRbSib1 & , (nRbSib1 - 1) \leq \left\lfloor \frac{|N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB}|}{2} \right\rfloor \
N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB} \times (N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB} - nRbSib1 + 1) + (N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB} - 1 - startRbSib1) & , (nRbSib1 - 1) > \left\lfloor \frac{|N\_{CORESET(0)}^{RB}|}{2} \right\rfloor
\end{cases}
$$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11471.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

The time domain resource allocation index for each SIB1 transmission is the one defined by the 5G-L2-PS during the PDSCH time domain resource allocation of the SIB1.

VRB-to-PRB mapping is set to Non-Interleaved (0).

The Modulation and Coding Scheme field is set to the value of IMCS computed according to the transport block size and coding rate expected for the SIB1 (see section “SIB1 initial transmission and retransmission pattern”).

The Redundancy version is set according to the transmission index of the SIB1 for a given SS/PBCH block configured (the first index is the initial transmission and the others the retransmissions) as follows.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Transmission index | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | 6 | 7 | 8 |
| Redundancy Version index | 0 | 2 | 3 | 1 | 0 | 2 | 3 | 1 |

The System information indicator is set to 0 for the SIB1 transmission.

---

### 3.22.4.11 SIB1 scheduling procedure

**3.22.4.11.0-1**  (ID: `11165512`)

SIB1 scheduling procedure
For each occurences of SFN and slot for SIB1 transmission, the 5G-L2 PS sends 3 messages to the 5G-L1-DL:

 The DlData\_PdcchSendReq.

 The DlData\_PdschSendReq.

 The DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq.

The SIB1 scheduling is done before any other PDCCH/PDSCH resource allocation. Moreover, other allocations overlapping the SIB1 resources are dropped in the slot handling the SIB1 (like CSI-RS for tracking...).

When there is only one SIB1 scheduled in a slot, then the 3 messages are always sent to one subcell.

When there are two SIB1 to be broadcasted in a given slot, each set of messages associated to SIB1 must be mapped to different subcell. In that case, at least 2 subcells must be available.

---

### 3.22.4.12 SIB1 error handling and successful configuration

#### 3.22.4.12.1 SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed

##### 3.22.4.12.1.0-1 SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed procedure (ID: 11165528)

**3.22.4.12.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12514667`)

SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
12514667:
SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
When the 5G-L2-PS receives the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq with a field “informationBlockType” set to “SystemInformationBlock”, the payload size is checked after the slot and multiplexing type selections. When the parameter “systemInformationTargetRate” is set to 1, the MCS0 will be used to restrict the TBS, otherwise the MCS9 3GPP maximum TBS for SI will be used to restrict the TBS allowed.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the payload size sent by the C-Plane according to the number of RB associated to the coreset(0), the smallest number of OFDM symbols of time domain allocation length saved in the SS/PBCH SIB1 context at the end of the multiplexing type selection process, the rate associated to the MCS0 or MCS9 according to the systemInformationTargetRate (see above).

On the 5G-L2-PS side, the information received in PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq are not taken into account and the SIB1 passive context is not valid and could not become active, when the check, detailed hereafter, is failed.

The first step is to compute the intermediate TBS (*TBS*min) as follows.\*\*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines `TBSmin` in two parts.
The first part is:
`TBSmin = | (NRE × (nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging) × RMcs) / 2n+9 | × 2n`
The second part, which is conditional on `n`, is:
`= max(3, | Log2 ( (NRE × nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging × RMcs) / 2^9 ) | - 6)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11478.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

With

*nRbCch:*

Number of Resource Block available for the coreset(0) part (24, 48 or 96) according to the value of the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Number of RB of the CORESET(0) bandwidth |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| SS/PBCH SCS (kHz) |  | 15 |  | 30 |  | 30 (n79[CB009173-B] and n104 [End CB009173-B]) |  | 120 |  | 240 |  |
| Common SCS (kHz) |  | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 60 | 120 | 60 | 120 |
| type0CoresetConfigurationIndex | 0 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 |
| 1 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 |  |
| 2 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 48 |  |
| 3 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 24 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 48 |  |
| 4 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 48 | 24 | - | 24 |  |
| 5 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 48 | 24 | - | 24 |  |
| 6 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 96 | 48 | - | 48 |  |
| 7 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 96 | 48 | - | 48 |  |
| 8 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 48 | - | - | - |  |
| 9 | 48 | 48 | - | 24 | - | 48 | 48 | - | - | - |  |
| 10 | 48 | 48 | - | 48 | - | - | 96 | - | - | - |  |
| 11 | 48 | 48 | - | 48 | - | - | 96 | - | - | - |  |
| 12 | 96 | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |  |
| 13 | 96 | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |  |
| 14 | 96 | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |  |
| 15 | - | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |  |

minRbReservedForNonSiPaging:

Minimum *number of RBs reserved for other UEs RNTI that could be used to scheduled using DCI 1\_0 format. (NIDD Parameter /NRBTS/NRCELL/minRbReservedForNonSiPaging)*

*Note:* if NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is False, then minRbReservedForNonSiPaging shall not be referred.\*\*

*N*RE:\*\*

Number of Resource Elements (RE) available per PRB. The 5G-L2-PS selects the SLIV with smallest length saved in the SS/PBCH SIB1 contexts at the end of the multiplexing type selection process. With the SLIV, the 5G-L2-PS identifies the number of RE per PRB to be used (see following table).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Default PDSCH Time domain resource allocation for SIB1 transmissions |  |  |  |  |  |
| SLIV Index | dmrsTypeAPosition | PDSCH mapping type | OFDM Start symbol (S) | Time domain length (L) | Number of RE per PRB |
| 1 | 2 | Type A | 2 | 12 | 108 |
| 3 | 3 | 11 | 96 |  |  |
| 2 | 2 | Type A | 2 | 10 | 84 |
| 3 | 3 | 9 | 72 |  |  |
| 3 | 2 | Type A | 2 | 9 | 72 |
| 3 | 3 | 8 | 60 |  |  |
| 4 | 2 | Type A | 2 | 7 | 60 |
| 3 | 3 | 6 | 48 |  |  |
| 5 | 2 | Type A | 2 | 5 | 48 |
| 3 | 3 | 4 | 36 |  |  |
| 6 | 2 | Type B | 9 | 4 | 36 |
| 3 | 10 | 4 |  |  |  |
| 7 | 2 | Type B | 4 | 4 | 36 |
| 3 | 6 | 4 |  |  |  |
| 8 | 2, 3 | Type B | 5 | 7 | 60 |
| 9 | 2, 3 | Type B | 5 | 2 | 18 |
| 10 | 2, 3 | Type B | 9 | 2 | 18 |
| 11 | 2, 3 | Type B | 12 | 2 | 18 |
| 12 | 2, 3 | Type A | 1 | 13 | 120 |
| 13 | 2, 3 | Type A | 1 | 6 | 60 |
| 14 | 2, 3 | Type A | 2 | 4 | 36 |
| 15 | 2, 3 | Type B | 4 | 7 | 60 |
| 16 | 2, 3 | Type B | 8 | 4 | 36 |

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "R MCS" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, purple, and yellow, and have a slight glow effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11478.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:

Target coding rate is set to 120 (MCS0) when the systemInformationTargetRate is set to 1, otherwise it is set to 679 (MCS9).

Then, the 5G-L2-PS gets the real TBS by selecting the closest TBS in the following list that is not less than the TBSmin computed previously and not greater than 2976 bits (maximum size of the Transport Block for a SI message defined by the 3GPP).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Index | TBS | Index | TBS | Index | TBS | Index | TBS |
| 1 | 24 | 31 | 336 | 61 | 1288 | 91 | 3624 |
| 2 | 32 | 32 | 352 | 62 | 1320 | 92 | 3752 |
| 3 | 40 | 33 | 368 | 63 | 1352 | 93 | 3824 |
| 4 | 48 | 34 | 384 | 64 | 1416 |  |  |
| 5 | 56 | 35 | 408 | 65 | 1480 |  |  |
| 6 | 64 | 36 | 432 | 66 | 1544 |  |  |
| 7 | 72 | 37 | 456 | 67 | 1608 |  |  |
| 8 | 80 | 38 | 480 | 68 | 1672 |  |  |
| 9 | 88 | 39 | 504 | 69 | 1736 |  |  |
| 10 | 96 | 40 | 528 | 70 | 1800 |  |  |
| 11 | 104 | 41 | 552 | 71 | 1864 |  |  |
| 12 | 112 | 42 | 576 | 72 | 1928 |  |  |
| 13 | 120 | 43 | 608 | 73 | 2024 |  |  |
| 14 | 128 | 44 | 640 | 74 | 2088 |  |  |
| 15 | 136 | 45 | 672 | 75 | 2152 |  |  |
| 16 | 144 | 46 | 704 | 76 | 2216 |  |  |
| 17 | 152 | 47 | 736 | 77 | 2280 |  |  |
| 18 | 160 | 48 | 768 | 78 | 2408 |  |  |
| 19 | 168 | 49 | 808 | 79 | 2472 |  |  |
| 20 | 176 | 50 | 848 | 80 | 2536 |  |  |
| 21 | 184 | 51 | 888 | 81 | 2600 |  |  |
| 22 | 192 | 52 | 928 | 82 | 2664 |  |  |
| 23 | 208 | 53 | 984 | 83 | 2728 |  |  |
| 24 | 224 | 54 | 1032 | 84 | 2792 |  |  |
| 25 | 240 | 55 | 1064 | 85 | 2856 |  |  |
| 26 | 256 | 56 | 1128 | 86 | 2976 |  |  |
| 27 | 272 | 57 | 1160 | 87 | 3104 |  |  |
| 28 | 288 | 58 | 1192 | 88 | 3240 |  |  |
| 29 | 304 | 59 | 1224 | 89 | 3368 |  |  |
| 30 | 320 | 60 | 1256 | 90 | 3496 |  |  |

The 5G-L2-PS compare the TBS obtained to the SIB1 payload size sent by the C-Plane.

If the payload size received does not fit the TBS, the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message is sent back to the C-Plane with the following content:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00000100.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follows:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is equal to the SLIV of the time domain resource allocation used.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is equal to the frequency domain resource allocation (it could be 24 or 48 or 96 RBs).

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is set to the Transport Block Size computed.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the SIB1 payload size received in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is set to the pwsType value associated to SIB1 payload size received in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq.

The “diagnosticInformation[5-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.22.4.12.1.0-2 SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed fault structure (ID: 11165593)

**3.22.4.12.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11165604`)

SIB1 payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00000100.

This cause indicates “Incorrect systemInformationTargetRate [CB009550-B] or minRbReservedForNonSiPaging [End CB009550-B] parameter setting for SIB1 transmissions”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]”elements reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message.

---

#### 3.22.4.12.2 SIB1 slot selection failure

##### 3.22.4.12.2.0-1 SIB1 slot selection failure procedure (ID: 11165634)

**3.22.4.12.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11165639`)

SIB1 slot selection failure
During the SIB1 slot selection process, the 5G-L2-PS defines the candidate slots to handle the SIB1 transmissions for each SS/PBCH configured.

When there is no slot candidate for a given SS/PBCH, the 5G-L2-PS stops the slot selection process and reports to the C-Plane the failure through the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message.

For each SS/PBCH configured, the 5G-L2-PS selects the two consecutive slots candidate for the SIB1 (n0, n0+1) and check that it is possible to allocate the SIB1 PDCCH and PDSCH resources time domain for the SS/PBCH selected.

To do the check, the 5G-L2-PS removes all symbols available before the PDCCH occasion associated to the SS/PBCH to check and its associated PDCCH symbols. Then 5G-L2-PS checks that at least one Time Domain Resource Allocation (SLIV, with more than 2 OFDM symbol length and PDSCH mapping type allowed) is valid for each candidate slot.

If no TDRA is valid on both slots, the 5G-L2-PS reports to the C-Plane, the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00000200.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follows:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is equal to the slot index in the radio frame for the first candidate slot.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is equal to the slot index in the radio frame for the second candidate slot.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is equal to the absolute SS/PBCH index associated to the candidate slots.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set according to the slot format or the type of signals/channel already present in the slot where the issue is detected:

 0x00000000: UL slot or Special slot without enough DL symbols.

 0x00000001: Slot with SS/PBCH.

 0x00000002: Slot with CSI-RS for tracking.

 0x00000003: Slot with CSI-RS for channel feedback.

 0x000000FF: Undefined.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.22.4.12.2.0-2 SIB1 slot selection failure fault structure (ID: 11165646)

**3.22.4.12.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165651`)

SIB1 slot selection failure
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00000200.

This cause indicates “Invalid slots for SIB1 due to incorrect SIB1 search space or frame structure or SS/PBCH configuration”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]”elements reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfo-ConfigurationResp message.

#### 3.22.4.12.3 Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages

##### 3.22.4.12.3.0-1 Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages procedure (ID: 11165671)

**3.22.4.12.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11165677`)

Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages
When the operator sets the systemInformationTargetRate parameter to a value not equal to 1, then the 5G-L2-PS computes the Link Adaptation settings to match the expected target rate. Nevertheless, according to the SIB1 payload size, the size of the Control Resource Set used for the SIB1 Downlink Control Information and the number of SS/PBCH configured it is possible that the expected target rate set by the operator is not the one obtained after several SIB1 transmissions.

When the systemInformationTargetRate parameter is set to 1, there is no discrepancy as the expected target rate and the one obtained is the same and is defined by the MCS used (MCS0).

For each SS/PBCH configured, the 5G-L2-PS computes the estimated rate after the number of SIB1 transmissions to find the parameters for the Link Adaptation of the associated SIB1 and compares it to the expected coding rate defined by the system information target rate (systemInformationTargetRate) when it is not equal to 0 or the one defined according to the Aggegation Level (AL) selected for the SI grant (dciSiAggregationLevel).

As the same LA characteristics are applied to SIB1 transmissions for a group of SS/PBCH, the 5G-L2-PS builds the bitmap of the SS/PBCH for each LA set.

Each LA set contains:

 The Modulation and Coding Scheme (MCS) used,

 The number of RB used.

 The number of RE per PRB used for the LA computation.

 The number of transmissions.

When the delta between the estimated rate after SIB1 transmissions and the rate defined by the “SystemInformationTargetRate” parameter is greater than a threshold defined hereafter according to the MCS used for the SIB1 transmissions, the 5G-L2-PS saves the data for up to the two first LA sets leading the discrepancy coverage detection to report them in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message. The 5G-L2-PS does not stop the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq processing for this discrepancy coverage detection. The threshold is set according to MCS computed for the LA set considered as follows.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Modulation and coding scheme | Threshold |
| 0 to 2 | 40 |
| 3 to 4 | 60 |
| 5 to 9 | 80 |

At the end of the processing, if there is no other error detected, the 5G-L2-PS reports to the C-Plane, the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “OK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00000300.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follows:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is the value of the rate used in the check (from systemInformationTargetRate and dciSiAggregationLevel parameters).

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is the 32 MSB of the SS/PBCH bitmap associated to the first LA set leading the coverage discrepancy.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is the 32 LSB of the SS/PBCH bitmap associated to the first LA set leading the coverage discrepancy.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is the concatenation of the estimated rate (2 most significant bytes) and the threshold (2 least significant bytes) used for the first LA set leading the coverage discrepancy.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is the concatenation of MCS (2 most significant bytes) and the number of RBs used (2 least significant bytes) for the first LA set leading the coverage discrepancy.

 The “diagnosticInformation[5]” element is the concatenation of number of SIB1 transmissions (2 most significant bytes) and the number of RE per PRBs (2 least significant bytes) used for the first LA set leading the coverage discrepancy.

 The “diagnosticInformation[6]” element is the 32 Most Significant Bits of the SS/PBCH bitmap associated to the second LA set leading the coverage discrepancy, if there is a second one. Otherwise the field is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[7]” element is the 32 Least Significant Bits of the SS/PBCH bitmap associated to the second LA set leading the coverage discrepancy, if there is a second one. Otherwise the field is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[8]” element is the concatenation of the estimated rate (2 most significant bytes) and the threshold (2 least significant bytes) used for the second LA set leading the coverage discrepancy, if there is a second one. Otherwise the field is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[9]” element is the concatenation of MCS (2 most significant bytes) and the number of RBs (2 least significant bytes) used for the second LA set leading the coverage discrepancy, if there is a second one. Otherwise the field is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[10]” element is the concatenation of number of SIB1 transmissions (2 most significant bytes) and the number of RE per PRBs (2 least significant bytes) used for the second LA set leading the coverage discrepancy, if there is a second one. Otherwise the field is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[11]” element is set to the pwsType value associated to failed SIB1 context.

The “diagnosticInformation[12-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.22.4.12.3.0-2 Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages fault structure (ID: 11165683)

**3.22.4.12.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165689`)

The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity): EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

This cause indicates “Discrepancy between configured and estimated SIB1 coverage”.

##### 3.22.4.12.3.0-3 Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages Additional text when FaultId_IncorrectCellParameterSetting (ID: 11165693)

**3.22.4.12.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11165699`)

Discrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coveragesDiscrepancy between the configured and estimated SIB1 coverages

Cause: Discrepancy between configured and estimated SIB1 coverage

targetRate:

nSib1Tx:

nRePerRb:

second Link Adaptation set:

ssPbchBitmap:

estimatedRate:

threshold:

mcs:

nRb:

nSib1Tx:

nRePerRb:

pwsType:

---

#### 3.22.4.12.4 Incorrect SIB1 configuration with Public Warning System

**3.22.4.12.4.0-1**  (ID: `11165711`)

Incorrect SIB1 configuration with Public Warning System
When the 5G-L2-PS receives a SIB1 configuration with a "pwsType" field not equal to 0 and the "modificationTimeFrame" set to "mibOrSiWindow", it sends back to the C-Plane a negative acknowledgement if there is no active or passive SIB1 context with a "pwsType" field equal to 0.

When the 5G-L2-PS receives no SIB1 configuration with a "pwsType" field equal to 0 and with the "modificationTimeFrame" set to "modificationPeriod", it sends back to the C-Plane a negative acknowledgement as detailed hereafter.

The PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message is sent with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00000500.

This cause indicates "Incorrect SIB1 configuration with Public Warning System".

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follows:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

#### 3.22.4.12.5 Default processing error report

##### 3.22.4.12.5.0-1 Default processing error report procedure (ID: 11165721)

**3.22.4.12.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11165726`)

Default processing error report
When the 5G-L2-PS detects any other error, it may or may not stop the processing according default defense procedure, but always reports the issue to the C-Plane through the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “OK” or “NOK”.

The expected status must be defined according to the expected behavior from the design point of view:

 If it is “OK”, then the configuration will be considered degraded by the C-Plane and a BTS fault will be raised to the fault services, but the cell will be degraded.

 If it is “NOK”, then the configuration will be considered as failed by the C-Plane and the cell will be not operational or degraded according to the cell context.

 The cause is set to 0x00000400.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array may be fulfilled with additional data defined by the design team.

---

##### 3.22.4.12.5.0-2 Default processing error report fault structure (ID: 11165731)

**3.22.4.12.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165737`)

Default processing error report
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00000400.

This cause indicates “Internal SIB1 processing error”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]”elements reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfo-ConfigurationResp message.

---

##### 3.22.4.12.5.0-3 Default processing error report additional text when FaultId_IncorrectCellParameterSetting (ID: 11165743)

**3.22.4.12.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11165746`)

Default processing error report
The additional text sent in the alarm by the gNB is detailed hereafter, when faultId is set to FaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting with the extraFaultInfo[0] set to 0x00000400.

All extraFaultInfo fields (1 to 13) are  grouped 4 by 4, in hexadecimal with the prefix "0x" and a space is added between each field.

Cause: Internal SIB1 processing error

dataDump :

## 3.22.5 System Information Messages Management

### 3.22.5.1 Maximum Transport Block Size for SI messages report at the cell setup

#### 3.22.5.1.0-1 Maximum Transport Block Size for SI messages report at the cell setup Determines TBS for SI (ID: 11165764)

**3.22.5.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12514676`)

Maximum Transport Block Size for SI messages report at the cell setup
12514676:
Maximum Transport Block Size for SI messages report at the cell setup
The 5G-L2-PS reports, in the PsCell\_CellSetupResp message, the maximum TBS (*siMsgTbsMax) that the cell configuration may handle on air interface for the SI message.*
This computation is done after the identification of the common Time Domain Resource Allocation list (reported in the same message and defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2388\_replaced([11115345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kptNHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the followings). From this list, the smallest length starting from the position of the front loaded DM-RS for PDSCH mapping type A (dmRsTypeAPosition) is selected.
The Frequency Domain Resource Allocation used to compute the maximum TBS is aligned to the CORESET(0) Bandwidth which is defined in the cell setup procedure.
Then the 5G-L2-PS applies the 2 folowing steps to get the maximum TBS allowed:
 Computation of the minimum TBS according to the resource allocation (TD and FD) and the maximum coding rate allowed for SI transmissions (679 corresponding to the MCS9.
 Extract the TBS from the 3GPP TBS table not lower to the minimum TBS computed previously and not greater than the maximum TBS allowed for the SI transmissions (2976 bits).
The computation is  detailed hereafter, by starting to get the minimum TBS (*TBS*min) as follows.**[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines $TBS\_{min}$ in two parts.
The first part is:
$TBS\_{min} = \left\lfloor \frac{N\_{RE} \times (nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging) \times R\_{MCS}}{2^{n+9}} \right\rfloor \times 2^n$, with $n$.
The second part is:
$= \max \left(3, \left\lfloor \log\_2 \left( \frac{N\_{RE} \times nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging \times R\_{MCS}}{2^9} \right) \right\rfloor - 6 \right)$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11512.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
With*nRbCch:*
Number of Resource Block available for the CORESET(0) bandwidth (24, 48 or 96) according to the value of the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter.

| *Note:* if NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is False, then minRbReservedForNonSiPaging parameter shall not be referred.\*\* |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| The number of RE available per PRB is computed as follows, with the number of OFDM symbol of the time domain allocation [image-1][image\_desc](SLIV_length)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11512.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1] selected. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| <8 | 1 |

### 3.22.5.2 Data management

#### 3.22.5.2.0-1 Data management SI message contexts (ID: 11165862)

**3.22.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11165883`)

Data management
11165883:
Data management
The 5G-L2-PS will manage a double buffering system for the active and inactive contexts of each System Information message (SI-Msg) received.

When the C-Plane sends the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq with SI message content, the 5G-L2-PS saves the following data in the inactive SI message context identified by the “systemInformationIndex” associated to SI-Msg description:

 The System Information payload.

 The activation trigger “ModificationTimeFrame”. The new SI message transmission could be activated at different time according to the criterion defined by C-Plane:

 The next SI-Window (mibOrSiWindow).

 The next Modification Period (modificationPeriod), after the detection of a complete Modification Period (MP) by the 5G-L2-PS.

 The periodicity (P). This is the boundary of the new SI message transmission cycle (with a new initial transmission and associated retransmissions of the active SI-Msg).

 The SI window (SIwindow) defining the duration of one SI message transmission cycle. All SI messages have the same SI window.

 The modification period defining the synchronization point for multiple SI modification. This data is common to all minimum system information (MIB/SIB1) and all SI-Messages

The detail of the activation timing of SI-Messages is same as SIB1 which specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3698\_replaced([11164124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktdruvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If the active SI message context is empty at the message reception, then the periodicity, the SIwindow of the inactive context and the current System Frame Number (SFN) are used to activate the SI message context at the next SI-Window.

Otherwise, the active SI message data (periodicity, SIwindow, MP) and the SFN are used to trigger the update of the SI-Msg context if needed.

Each context (active/passive) contains the set of data received from the C-Plane and computed by the 5G-L2-PS for defining the SI message transmission of each SS/PBCH configured [CB008285-E-UPD001], activated (nActivatedSsPbch) and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001].

When the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq contains at least one SI message with the activation trigger set to “modificationPeriod”, then this PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq contains all SI messages which will be active at the next full modification period. When the list is lower than the number active SI messages transmitted, then the SI messages not present in the list will be removed at the beginning of the new MP.

The PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq may contain up to 19 SI messages. The 5G-L2-PS manages up to 19 active and 19 passive SI-Msg contexts. The 5G-L2-PS uses the value of pwsType field on top of the SI message index  to differentiate the SI-Msg active and passive contexts. Only up to 3 SI-Msg indexes could have a pwsType value not equal to 0, according to the PWS processing. When a SI-Msg is configured with a pwsType value not equal to 0, it is not mandatory to have another context for this SI-Msg with the pwsType set to 0. In that case, the PWS SIB is alone in the SI-Msg and the SI-Msg is not transmitted at all when the PWS SIB is not broadcasted (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3872\_replaced([11166942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktoDyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and followings).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to system information configuration. The flowchart begins with a request labeled "PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq(n x SI-Msg)".
The process then enters a loop indicated by "n x" on the left side, suggesting it will be repeated 'n' times. Inside this loop, the following steps occur:
1. **Update passive context with received data**: This is the first step within the loop.
2. **SI-Msg[n] initial transmission and retransmission pattern definition**: This step defines the transmission patterns for SI-Msg[n].
3. **Update passive context with data of SI-Msg[n] pattern definition**: The passive context is updated with information from the defined pattern.
Following these steps, there is a decision point:
\* **Is active SI-Msg[n] context empty?**: This is a diamond-shaped decision box.
\* If the answer is **No**, the process proceeds to the "End" state.
\* If the answer is **Yes**, the process moves to the next step: **Update periodicity and SI window size in active SI-Msg[n] context**. After this update, the process also proceeds to the "End" state.
The flowchart concludes with an "End" state, represented by an oval shape.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11516.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

#### 3.22.5.2.0-2 Data management Several types of a SI-Msg management (ID: 11165890)

**3.22.5.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11165897`)

Data management
When the 5G-L2-PS manages several configurations of a given SI-Msg (up to 2, according to the PWS data), the 5G-L2-PS selects the expected SI-Msg among the SI-Msg active contexts according to to the processing of the PWS messages and detailed in the Public Warning System management section (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3872\_replaced([11166942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktoDyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and followings).

---

#### 3.22.5.2.0-3 Data management SI passive context overwriting (ID: 11165901)

**3.22.5.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11165908`)

Data management
Since there is only 1 passive buffer for each SI message, 5G-L2-PS is not expect to receive new SystemInformationConfigurationReq message when the previous request is not activated.

If such case happens, the new request will overwrite the old request in the passive buffer, and the old request will be lost.

---

### 3.22.5.3 Broadcasted SI message initial transmission and retransmissions pattern

**3.22.5.3.0-1**  (ID: `11165918`)

Broadcasted SI message initial transmission and retransmissions pattern
Each SI message configured and broadcasted, has a specific Time Domain area (start system frame number, start slot within the radio frame and duration) which avoids SI window overlapping between two different SI messages and the need to manage the multiplexing different SI messages within the same slot.

The periodicity of SI messages and the size of the SI window allow to avoid the need of multiplexing a SI message for two different SS/PBCH configured within the slot even if by configuration there are several PDCCH occasions per slot defined for the PDCCH type 0A (assuming the type 0A PDCCH does not used the search space defined for the SIB1).

Of course, the time for the whole SI messages acquisition will be increased without multiplexing (TD/FD) within the slot and according to the PDSCH allocation for a given SI message.

To define the TD scheduling of each SI message and each SS/PBCH configured, the 5G-L2-PS applies the following steps:

 PDSCH resources and Transport Block computation.

 Expected coverage of SI message.

 Slot selection for the number of expected SI message transmissions and for each SS/PBCH configured.

---

#### 3.22.5.3.1 PDSCH resources and Transport Block computation

##### 3.22.5.3.1.1 Time Domain Resource Allocation selection

###### 3.22.5.3.1.1.0-1 Time Domain Resource Allocation selection Check common PDSCH Time Domain Resource Allocation (TDRA) list (ID: 11165937)

**3.22.5.3.1.1.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13424243`)

Time Domain Resource Allocation selection
The time domain allocations available for the SI messages transmision is defined according to the common PDSCH Time Domain Resource Allocation (TDRA) computed at the cell setup (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6667\_replaced([11115365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpt0IfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The 5G-L2-PS selects several valid configurations according to the definition of the PDCCH and the candidate OFDM symbols for the Channel State Information Reference Signal (CSI-RS) booked for the channel state feedback (last ofdm symbol) in order to maximize the PDSCH allocation for all potential sizes of the PDCCH in the initial bandwidth part.

For FDD: The SI messages will use only the slots with the largest number of OFDM symbols allocated to the downlink.

With the position of the DM-RS for the PDSCH Type A allocation received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq, the 5G-L2-PS selects the time domain resource allocations as follows:

 The TDRA allowing PDSCH mapping type A with a SLIV using the start OFDM symbol defined by the front-loaded DM-RS Type A position and the largest length available which does not include the OFDM symbols for the CSI-RS transmissions.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Allowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OFDM symbols used for any kind of CSI-RS transmissions in any of the CsiRsPoolingGroup shall also be excluded. When slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE, a list of such symbols is determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19557\_replaced([11115143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kprX5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB013525-D] If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode = 1 (mute\_slot\_3\_6\_8)

The last OFDM symbol in slot offsets 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall also be excluded

Else If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode = 2 (mute\_slot\_0\_3\_6\_8)

The last OFDM symbol in slot offsets 0, 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall also be excluded

End If

[CB013525-D]  If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode is not 0 (0: disabled or not configured), symbols in slots defined in ([11115176: Determine slots allocated to CSI-RS for Channel Measurements Slots in other CsiRsPoolingGroups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall not be used for any SI transmission irrespective of the ZAB privilege of the cell.

[End CB013525-D]

This TDRA will be use as the initial TDRA to compute the SI-Msg Link Adaptation parameters and especially the TBS which must be constant for all transmissions of a given SI-Msg.

 When the parameter “SystemInformationTargetRate” is not set to 1, the other TDRAs allowing PDSCH mapping type A with all SLIV defined in the common PDSCH Time Domain Resource Allocation.

These TDRA are used in order to accommodate the frequency domain allocation to keep the same TBS and MCS with a selected TDRA not equal to the initial one.

For TDD: Maximum PDSCH allocation shall be calcualted based on the smallest *SLIV*Length  in common time domain resource allocation (TDRA) list. This TDRA will be use as the initial TDRA to compute the SI-Msg Link Adaptation parameters and especially the TBS which must be constant for all transmissions of a given SI-Msg.\*\*

When the parameter “SystemInformationTargetRate” is not set to 1, the other TDRAs allowing PDSCH mapping type A with all SLIV defined in the common PDSCH Time Domain Resource Allocation. These TDRA are used in order to accommodate the frequency domain allocation to keep the same TBS and MCS with a selected TDRA not equal to the initial one.

The allowed time domain resource allocations are saved in the passive context of the SI messages. If there is no available time domain allocation compatible with those constraints, the 5G-L2-PS considers the system information configuration request as not successful.

---

###### 3.22.5.3.1.1.0-2 Time Domain Resource Allocation selection Check Target Coding Rate for TD allocation (ID: 11165975)

**3.22.5.3.1.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `12874669`)

Time Domain Resource Allocation selection
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1allowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall always allocate only TD resources which do not use the symbols reserved for any kind of CSI-RS in any CsiRsPoolingGroup (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2511\_replaced([11116693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp6BcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for initial/first transmission.

If "SystemInformationTargetRate" is not equal to 1,

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1allowed = FALSE and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* 5G-L2-PS will try to allocate the largest possible length in time domain when it schedules a SI message transmission (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3825\_replaced([11166424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), whether it is the initial transmission or the retransmission.

Else

* 5G-L2-PS will try to allocate the largest possible length in time domain when it schedules a SI message transmission (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3825\_replaced([11166424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for non initial transmission.

If the cell is not granted ZAB privilege by the BBRM in the current Pooling period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [**CB014543-H,**CB014543-G] ,[ Note: w**hen partial ZAB is enabled (partialZABAllowed = True), the BBRM determines the set of ZAB-privileged cells according to the specification in ([12804289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ui5xYp6QEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). This privilege assignment may subsequently be overridden by the algorithm detailed in ([12825840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Onwec61_EfCyQasEtWkQ4A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))],**[End CB014543-H,***\*CB014543-G]***\*

* The DL symbols reserved for any kind of CSI-RS in any csirsPoolingGroup cannot be used.

Else

* All PDSCH symbols can be used.

End If

End If

[Before CB013525-D] If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode = 1 (mute\_slot\_3\_6\_8);

* The last DL symbols in slot offsets 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall not be used for any SI transmission irrespective of the ZAB privilege of the cell.

Else If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode = 2 (mute\_slot\_0\_3\_6\_8);

* The last DL symbols in slot offsets 0, 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall not be used for any SI transmission irrespective of the ZAB privilege of the cell.

End If

[CB013525-D]  If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode is not 0 (0: disabled or not configured), symbols in slots defined in ([11115176: Determine slots allocated to CSI-RS for Channel Measurements Slots in other CsiRsPoolingGroups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall not be used for any SI transmission irrespective of the ZAB privilege of the cell. [End CB013525-D]

* 5G-L2-PS shall find out the FD allocation for this TD allocation to make sure the Transport Block Size is same as the one calculated with the initial TD allocation. (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3798\_replaced([11165937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjLTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the initial TD allocation and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16704\_replaced([11166021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the Transport Block size calculation).

If 5G-L2-PS fails to find out such FD allocation to keep the same Transport Block size, then the initial TD allocation will be used for this transmission.

Else

* 5G-L2-PS will always use the initial TD allocation for the SI message transmission.

End If
