##### 3.22.5.3.1.2 Frequency Domain allocation and Transport Block Size

###### 3.22.5.3.1.2.0-1 Frequency Domain allocation and Transport Block Size Transport Block Calculation (ID: 11166021)

**3.22.5.3.1.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12514697`)

Frequency Domain allocation and Transport Block Size
12514697:
Frequency Domain allocation and Transport Block Size
The 5G-L2-PS with the time domain allocations defined for each SI-Msg in the previous steps, applies the following algorithm to identify a set of Link Adaption parameters for each SI-Msg associated to SS/PBCH configured.
When several time domain allocations are allowed, the 5G-L2-PS selects first, among the list of allowed time domain allocations, the initial TDRA. With this one, the 5G-L2-PS computes the Link Adaptation parameters. For the other time domain allocations saved in the SI message context, the 5G-L2-PS will compute the number of RB needed to get the same TBS with the same coding rate computed with the initial TDRA.
According to the value of the parameter “SystemInformationTargetRate”, the 5G-L2-PS has 2 behaviors:
 When the parameter is not equal to 1, number of RB for the SI message ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "nRbStMsgn". The text is blurry and appears to be in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11540.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]) is set to the size of the CORESET(0) bandwidth (24 or 48 or 96) defined by the "type0CoresetConfigurationIndex" parameter according to the SCS (common and SS/PBCH) and the operating band minus minimum PRB reserved for other RNTIs defined by "minRbReservedForNonSiPaging"([image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "nRbCc.ch – minRbReservedForNonSiPaging". The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The font appears to be a sans-serif font. The text is slightly blurry, but it is still legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11540.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]). 5G-L2-PS then to compute the size of the PDSCH resources (in time and frequency domains), the 5G-L2-PS scans the different target coding rates with all possible sizes of PRB allocation to identify whole combinations allowed by using the constraints hereafter.
 If the parameter “SystemInformationTargetRate” is set to 1, the number of RB for the SI message ([image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "nRbStMsgn". The text is blurry and appears to be in a light gray color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11540.001.png[/image\_path][/image-2]) is set to the size of the CORESET(0) bandwidth (24 or 48 or 96) defined by the “type0CoresetConfigurationIndex” parameter according to the SCS (common and SS/PBCH) and the operating band. The 5G-L2-PS identifies the coding rate (R) and the Modulation and Coding Scheme (MCS) handling the SI-Msg size by using the constraints hereafter.
The combination to handle the SI-Msg(n) or the set of them are identified by the following constraints.
 
[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula presented in a piecewise format, indicated by the curly brace on the left. The formula defines a condition for `TBSsiMsg(n)(index)`.
The main condition is:
`TBSsiMsg(n)(index) ≥ |NRE × nRbSiMsg_n × RMCS / 2^(n+9)| × 2^n`
This condition is further qualified by:
`with n = max(3, |Log2((NRE × nRbSiMsg_n × RMCS) / 2^9)| - 6)`
Additionally, there are two sub-conditions:
1. `TBS(index) ≥ siMsg_n,size`
2. `1 ≤ nRbSiMsg_n ≤ nRbCch`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11540.003.png[/image\_path][/image-3]
  
With
*nRbCch:*
Number of Resource Block available for the SI-Messages (24, 48 or 96) according to the value of the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter.

The number of RE available per PRB is computed as follows, with the characteristics of the time domain allocation, the number of OFDM symbol of the time domain allocation [image-5][image\_desc](SLIV_length)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11540.005.png[/image\_path][/image-5].

[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation defining "duration". The equation is presented as a piecewise function.

The second case, when `dDmrsMappingType = TypeB`, defines `duration` as `SLIV_length`.

#### 3.22.5.3.2 Expected coverage of SI message

##### 3.22.5.3.2.0-1 Expected coverage of SI message (ID: 12825036)

**3.22.5.3.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12810352`)

Expected coverage of SI message
12810352:
Expected coverage of SI message
The SI message expected coverage is controlled by the number of RB allocated, the selected MCS and the number of retransmissions within the SI window. To manage it, several options are available according to the value of the parameter “SystemInformationTargetRate” under MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL object:

 When the parameter is equal to 0, then the SI-Msg PDSCH expected coverage, at the end of the SI window, is aligned to expected coverage of the PDCCH defined by the Aggregation Level used for the SI message grant (dciSiAggregationLevel).

 When the parameter is equal to 1, the SI messages are transmitted only once per SI Window and uses the whole RB of CORESET(0) bandwidth.

 Otherwise, the 5G-L2-PS selects the best combination of number of RBs, MCS and number of transmissions to reach the performance defined by the parameter.

When the system information target rate is not equal to 1 and after the computation of the PDSCH resource allocations in time and frequency domains with the associated MCS, the 5G-L2-PS must compute, for each combination, the equivalent coding rate after each retransmission as follows.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation presented as a piecewise function. The equation defines a variable $R\_{MCS,nbOfReTxSiMsg}$ based on the value of $nbOfReTxSiMsg$.
The function has two cases:
Case 1: If $nbOfReTxSiMsg = 0$, then $R\_{MCS,nbOfReTxSiMsg} = R\_{MCS}$.
Case 2: If $1 \leq nbOfReTxSiMsg \leq 8$, then $R\_{MCS,nbOfReTxSiMsg} = \frac{R\_{MCS}}{\sum\_{n=1}^{nbOfReTxSiMsg} 10^{0.24 \times n^{-s}}}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11542.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

With

*R*MCS:\*\*

Target coding rate define according to the modulation and coding scheme field used by the UE to identify the TBS transmit by the gNB (mcsSiMsgn).

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Modulation and coding scheme (mcsSiMsgn) | Target coding Rate (RMCS) |
| 0 | 120 |
| 1 | 157 |
| 2 | 193 |
| 3 | 251 |
| 4 | 308 |
| 5 | 379 |
| 6 | 449 |
| 7 | 526 |
| 8 | 602 |
| 9 | 679 |

From the initial transmission to the maximum transmission allowed and detailed hereafter, the selection of the combination (RB, MCS) is done by using the first smallest gap between the rate according to the maximum number of transmissions (maxTxSiMsg) defined hereafter and the expected coding rate defined by the system information target rate (SystemInformationTargetRate) when it is not equal to 0 or the one defined according to the AL selected for the SI grant (dciSiAggregationLevel) in the following table.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| dciSiAggregationLevel | Target coding Rate (R) |
| 4 | 140 |
| 8 | 70 |
| 16 | 35 |

The maximum number of transmissions is defined as follows:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in text. The formula defines a piecewise function `maxTxSiMsg` with two conditions.
The first condition is `nrLteDssMode ≤ 1`, which is associated with the value `8`. This condition is followed by `[CB007372-A-UPD001] or NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true [End CB007372-A-UPD001]`.
The second condition is `nrLteDssMode > 1`, which is associated with the value `2`. This condition is followed by `[CB007372-A-UPD001] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A-UPD001]`.
The text is presented in a mathematical notation style, with the variable `maxTxSiMsg` on the left side of an equals sign, followed by a curly brace indicating a piecewise definition. The conditions and their corresponding values are listed vertically. Some parts of the text are underlined with a dotted red line, suggesting they might be specific identifiers or parameters.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10171057.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[CB007372-A-UPD001] maxTxSiMsg for asymmetric DSS (NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true) shall be the same as for FDD non-DSS [End CB007372-A-UPD001]

For the other time domain allocations allowed, the 5G-L2-PS computes the number of RE for the PDSCH and searches the number of RB for each of them to get the same TBS with the rate used for the initial transmission (RMCS).

The 5G-L2-PS, for each time domain allowed in the previous steps and at the end of the Link Adaptation process, saves in the SI-Msg context the time domain allocation, the number of RB (nRbSiMsgSLIV) according to the time domain allowed, the number of transmissions and the MCS for each SI-Msg associated to the SS/PBCH configured.

---

#### 3.22.5.3.3 Slot selection for SI message transmissions

##### 3.22.5.3.3.0-1 Slot selection for SI message transmissions PDCCH occasion identification (ID: 11166178)

**3.22.5.3.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11166313`)

Slot selection for SI message transmissions
11166313:
Slot selection for SI message transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS identifies the PDCCH occasions within the SI window for each SI message received from the C-Plane according to the PDCCH type 0A configuration received at the cell setup, the index of the SI message, the SI window duration and the slot format within the slot pattern (rrmSlotPattern) computed at the cell setup.
For a given SI messge index, the first associated SI window is starting at the SFN and radio frame slot offsets as follows and will be repeated every periods defined for this SI message.
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation defines two variables, `sfnoffset` and `rfSlotOffset`, based on `siWindow` and `siMsgIndex`.
The equation is as follows:
$siWindow\_{siMsgIndex} = \begin{cases} sfnoffset = \left\lfloor \frac{siMsgIndex \times siWindow}{N\_{slot}^{frame,\mu}} \right\rfloor \ rfSlotOffset = (siMsgIndex \times siWindow) \mod N\_{slot}^{frame,\mu} \end{cases}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
With
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "stMsgIndex" in a light gray color against a white background. The text is slightly blurred, but all characters are legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:
System Information index received in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq.
[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "stWindows" in a blurry, light gray font against a white background. The text is slightly pixelated and has a subtle blue and yellow halo effect around the letters.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]:
System Information window duration received in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq.
[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "μ and N\_slot^frame,μ". The text is in a light blue color against a white background. The font is a sans-serif font. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]:
Numerology (µ) and number of slot per frame ([image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N\_{slot}^{frame, \mu}". The text is blurry and appears to be a mathematical expression.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]) according to the common SCS defined in the MIB.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Common SCS (kHz) | Numerology | slots per frame |
| 15 | 0 | 10 |
| 30 | 1 | 20 |
| 60 | 2 | 40 |
| 120 | 3 | 80 |
|  |  |  |
| For the SFN and RF slots within the SI window, the 5G-L2-PS checks the presence of the PDCCH occasion(s) which are not overlapping uplink symbols. |  |  |
| The PDCCH occasions within a slot are defined by the number of symbols activated in each slot through the monitoringSymbolWithinSlot parameter of the search space used for the SI message transmissions (Type0A-PDCCH). |  |  |
| The search space for SI message is starting when the following condition is met and for the consecutive slots defined by the Search Space duration. |  |  |
| When the following formula is verified, then the slot handles the PDCCH occasions for the downlink OFDM symbol defined through the monitoringSymbolWithinSlot. |  |  |
| [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: |  |  |
| $$(sfn \times 2^\mu \times 10 + rfSlot - slotOffset\_{ts}) - periodicity\_s \times \left\lfloor \frac{sfn \times 2^\mu \times 10 + rfSlot - slotOffset\_{ts}}{periodicity\_s} \right\rfloor < duration\_s$$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11546.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] |  |  |
| With |  |  |
| [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "sfn" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, orange, and yellow, and appear to have a slight blur or glow effect. ##### 3.22.5.3.3.0-2 Slot selection for SI message transmissions Eligible slot selection within the SI window (ID: 11166320)

**3.22.5.3.3.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `13253193`)

Slot selection for SI message transmissions
The 5G-L2-PS checks for each PDCCH occasions in the SI window, whether the slot is eligible for the SI transmission according to the following constraints and counts the number of available PDCCH occasions per SS/PBCH configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_83\_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 The slot has the highest DL capacity (DL14 for semi static frame structure or BI12,1 for flexible frame structure in TDD or any slot for FDD).

 The slot is not configured to handle the SS/PBCH configured,

 The slot is not configured to handle the CSI-RS for tracking when the reference signals overlap the PDSCH area aligned to the CORESET used for the SI message transmissions.

 If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True and actTddCsirsOpt is false, or (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is true and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false), or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the slots is configured to handle the CSI-RS for tracking in any cells of the pool are not allowed for SI-Msg transmission. The list of such slots handling the CSI-RS for tracking for all cells in the pool is determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11311\_replaced([11116871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp72kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11874\_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TDD and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19560\_replaced([11115160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kprX7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FDD.

 If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True and actTddCsirsOpt is false, or (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is true and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false), the slots, configured to handle Cell-Specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition for which there is no TDRA configured to handle the SI-Msg transmission in any cells of the pool, are not allowed. The list of such slots handling the Cell-Specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition is determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11311\_replaced([11116871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp72kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11874\_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the slots configured to handle Cell-Specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition of other CsiRsPoolingGroups (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19561\_replaced([11115176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) can handle SI-Msg transmissions. For such slots, if the cell has been granted ZAB privilege (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode **= 0 (i.e. the parameter is disabled and not configured), the** [Before CB013525-D] last symbol [CB013525-D] CSI-RS symbol [End CB013525-D] of the slot can be used for SI Msg transmission. In any other situation, such slots can be used as long as a valid SLIV exists where the last symbol is not used for PDSCH transmission.

* If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and CSI-IM is scheduled in the same symbol as CSI-RS for channel acquisition, the slots configured to handle Cell-Specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition of the cell's own CsiRsPoolingGroup (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19535\_replaced([11115109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kprX4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) can handle SI-Msg transmissions as long as a valid SLIV exists where the [Before CB013525-D] last symbol [CB013525-D] CSI-RS symbol [End CB013525-D] is not used for PDSCH transmission.
* If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and**CSI-IM is scheduled on symbol other than CSI-RS for channel acquisition, the slots configured to handle Cell-Specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition of the cell's own CsiRsPoolingGroup (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19535\_replaced([11115109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kprX4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be considered for SI-Msg transmissions.**
* For FDD non DSS cell, **if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is False, slots where** CSI-IM is scheduled on symbol other than CSI-RS for channel acquisition.\*\*\*\*
* [Before CB013525-D] If **NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode** **= 1 (mute\_slot\_3\_6\_8)**

The last symbol in slot offsets 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall not be used for any downlink  message transmissions. Hence, such slots can be used as long as a valid SLIV exists where the last symbol is not used for PDSCH transmission

Else If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode **= 2 (mute\_slot\_0\_3\_6\_8)**

The last symbol in slot offsets 0, 3 & 6 of every even SFN and slot offset 8 of every odd SFN shall not be used for any downlink  message transmissions. Hence, such slots can be used as long as a valid SLIV exists where the last symbol is not used for PDSCH transmission

End If [CB013525-D]  If NRBTS.slowPrbPoolFddFr1EnhCompMode is not 0 (disabled or not configured), symbols in slots defined in [11115176: Determine slots allocated to CSI-RS for Channel Measurements Slots in other CsiRsPoolingGroups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) shall not be used for any PDSCH transmission. Hence, such slots can be used as long as a valid SLIV exists where the impacted symbols are excluded. [End CB013525-D]

* The slot is not configured to handle SIB1 transmissions ([12827070: SIB1 candidate slots not allowed for other CCCH](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bCX9sa3PEfCyQasEtWkQ4A)) for the SS/PBCH configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_83\_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The slot is not configured to handle Paging transmissions for the SS/PBCH configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_83\_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 When NRCELL.actInfTddFrameMuting is set to true, the slot must not correspond to a muted slot (DL slot in the source cell corresponding to an UL slot in the target cell with another frame structure).

If NIDD actCsirsMultiplexing is false and If needReturnCsirs in PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq is false, the slot is not configured to handle cell specific CSI-RS transmissions for dlMimoMode 'CL 8x4 MIMO'.

Note: If NIDD actCsirsMultiplexing is true, cell specific CSI-RS can multiplex with OSI/paging within the same slot, so OSI slot does not need to exclude CSI-RS slot.

* If the cell is configured with TD-LTE frame structure using tdLteConfig0,
* channel BWs 10-15MHz: the last 2 consecutive DL slots in every 10 slots starting from slot offset 0 of the rrmSlotPattern (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) i.e. slot offsets 2, 3, 12, & 13 in every SFN
* For other channel BWs:  the last DL slot in every 10 slots starting from slot offset 0 of the rrmSlotPattern (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) i.e. slot offsets 3 & 13 in every SFN.

For each SI-Msg contexts and each SS/PBCH configured, activated and not muted, the 5G-L2-PS selects a set of candidate slots for which the PDCCH occasion indexes is for the SS/PBCH index (see above).

For each SI-Msg context received, if at least one transmission is allowed per SS/PCH configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_83\_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , then the SI message configuration is successful. Then the number of transmissions for a given SI-Msg, whatever the SS/PBCH considered (configured, activated and not muted), stored in the SI-Msg context will be restricted by the smallest number of transmissions allowed for a given SS/PBCH configured, activated and not muted.

When the available transmissions for a given SI-Msg is larger than the number of transmissions expected, the 5G-L2-PS restricts the number of transmissions to the one defined by the expected coverage of SI-Msg.

When the number of allowed transmissions is lower than the one expected, the 5G-L2-PS runs the LA process to get the best LA parameters according to the number of transmissions allowed.

In case L2-PS is not able to determine any valid occasions for the SI Msg transmission, an error should be raised and handled as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3847\_replaced([11166604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktmOl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note: in this artifact, actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator.**

---

##### 3.22.5.3.3.0-3 Slot selection for SI message transmissions Determination of slots for SI message transmission (ID: 11166365)

**3.22.5.3.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11166378`)

Slot selection for SI message transmissions
When determining the slots that are used for the SI message transmission according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3805\_replaced([11166178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktkZYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23573\_replaced([11166320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktkZZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall consider the rrmSlotPattern (for DL slot format, SS/PBCH slots and tracking CSI-RS slots), SIB1 transmission pattern and paging pattern.

The period of rrmSlotPattern is rrmSlotPatternLength.

The period of SIB1 transmission is "minPeriod" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3716\_replaced([11164922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kte50_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with max value 40ms.

The period of paging can be got from N value for paging which is defined in NIDD parameter MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/numOfPagingFrames . E.g. halfT means period = 2 radio frames, oneSixteenthT means period = 16 radio frames.

For each pattern considered, if the period is smaller than SI-periodicity, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the slot that need to excluded from SI message scheduling in the first SI-window. If the period is larger than SI-periodicity, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate all the SI-windows that are overlap with first period of considered pattern, and then map the result into single SI-window. E.g. if there is one slot should be excluded in the 2nd SI-window, it is also excluded in the 1st SI-window.

The final calculation result is all available slots for SI-message transmission within one SI-window and will be used by the later steps.

Note, for the above calculation about SIB1, if there is data in SIB1 passive buffer (pending for activation, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29006\_replaced([11164088](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktdrtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall used the confguration in SIB1 passive buffer, otherwise, the configuration in SIB1 active buffer s used.

5G-L2-PS shall go through all the available PDCCH occasions (in available slots) in a single SI-window from the start of the SI-window, and assign the SI message transmission for the corresponding beam (SS/PBCH) [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] except SS/PBCH corresponding to muted beams [CB008285-E] or to deactivated SS/PBCH (according to 5G\_UP\_7805\_replaced([11347149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa4fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB008285-E][CB008285-E-UPD001] configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_82\_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001]. 5G-L2-PS shall record the number of already assigned transmission for each beam. When the assigned number is reached the target number of transmission (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3803\_replaced([11166166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall not assign more transmission for that beam. This procedure end when all the beams  [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] except SS/PBCH corresponding to muted beams [CB008285-E] or to deactivated SS/PBCH (according to 5G\_UP\_7805\_replaced([11347149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa4fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB008285-E][CB008285-E-UPD001] (SS/PBCH) configured, activated and not muted (see 5G\_UP\_83\_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] are assigned with target transmission number.

If monitoringSymbolWithinSlot indicate more than 1 symbol can be used in 1 slot, 5G-L2-PS shall select the beam which has the least nunmber of already assigned transmission to transmit in this slot. If there are more than 1 beams which have same least number, it depends on implementation to choose one from them.

---

### 3.22.5.4 PDCCH resource allocation for the SI messages

#### 3.22.5.4.1 Control Channel Element start index

**3.22.5.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11166392`)

Control Channel Element start index
When the number of Control Channel Elements (CCE) and the number of candidates configured in the Type0A PDCCH allow several positions of the PDCCH candidate for SI-Msg PDCCH allocation, the 5G-L2-PS uses alternatively each of them across the SI window according to the CCE distribution between DL and UL schedulers.

The CCE start positions for each Aggregation Level (AL) allowed are defined below according to the combinations of PRB and OFDM symbol associated to the value of type0CoresetConfigurationIndex.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | CCE start positions |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Aggregation Level | AL4 |  |  |  | AL8 |  | AL16 |
|  | PDCCH candidate | 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 0 | 1 | 0 |
| CORESET configuration | {24,1} | 0 | - | - | - | - | - | - |
| {24,2} | 0 | 4 | - | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {24,3} | 0 | 4 | 8 | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {48,1} | 0 | 4 | - | - | 0 | - | - |  |
| {48,2} | 0 | 4 | 8 | 12 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {48,3} | 0 | 4 | 12 | 16 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {96,1} | 0 | 4 | 8 | 12 | 0 | 8 | 0 |  |
| {96,2} | 0 | 8 | 16 | 24 | 0 | 16 | 0 |  |
| {96,3} | 0 | 12 | 24 | 36 | 0 | 24 | 0 |  |

---

#### 3.22.5.4.2 Aggregation Level selection

##### 3.22.5.4.2.0-1 Aggregation Level selection (ID: 13337530)

**3.22.5.4.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13132726`)

Aggregation Level selection
The Aggregation selected for the SI-Msg transmissions is defined by the operator through the NIDD dciSiAggregationLevel parameter. [Before CB014330-F] It is transmitted to the 5G-L2-PS in the psCell\_CellSetupReq. [End CB014330-F]

---

#### 3.22.5.4.3 Other parameters for the PDCCH SI-Msg transmissions

### 3.22.5.5 PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages

#### 3.22.5.5.0-1 PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages Time domain allocation (ID: 11166424)

**3.22.5.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166429`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
For the target slot, the 5G-L2-PS identifies the PDSCH symbols allowed according to the PDCCH size (see PDCCH slot pattern management: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3958\_replaced([11168909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the unavailable symbols at the end of the slot (CSI-RS...). Then, The 5G-L2-PS selects, among the combinations of symbols and RBs saved in the SI-Msg context (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3799\_replaced([11165975](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the one which maximizes the PDSCH symbol usage for this slot.

---

#### 3.22.5.5.0-2 PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages Frequency domain allocation (ID: 11166434)

**3.22.5.5.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `12816258`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
For the target slot, gNB-DU selects the expected number of RBs associated to the SLIV selected previously (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3825\_replaced([11166424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If NRCELL.sibStartPrbRandomDisabled is set to True,

* Starting PRB of the SI-Msg shall be set to start PRB of coreset# 0

Else,

* The starting PRB index of the SI-Msg (startRbSiMsg) in a slot is computed randomly within the following range:
* PRBmin = 0.
* PRBmax = CORESET(0) size - 1 - nRbSiMsgSLIV.
* The random function is initialized with the Physical Cell Identity of the cell.

If /NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is set to True and if NRCELL.sibStartPrbRandomDisabled then randomly computed start PRB index shall be adjusted to multiples of minRBReservedForNonSiPaging (/NRBTS/NRCELL/minRBReservedForNonSiPaging)

When the DCI 1\_0 for the common channel (SIB1, SI , PAGING), rach msg2, rach msg4 are mapped on CORESET 0 but the DCI 1\_0 in CSS mode for transient phase (Type3 PDCCH CSS , see 38.213 §10.1) are mapped on a CORESET#X (with X>0) (and not on CORESET #0, see 5G\_UP\_10874\_replaced([11350654](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubnt5vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and when the start Prb of the CORESET 0 is lower than the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0),

if the highest PRB of SI-Msg is lower the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0), gNB-DU shall increment the starting PRB of the SI-Msg in order that there is no gap between SI-Msg and the CORESET#X (with X>0) PRBs area, that is the PRB above the highest PRB of SI-Msg is the start Prb of the CORESET#X (with X>0).

When NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true and **[Before CB015668-A]** NRBTS.actTddCsiRsOpt = true and NRBTS.actTddCsiImRm = true **[CB015668-A]**actTddCsiRsOpt = true and actTddCsiImRm = true (note: actTddCsirsOpt and actTddCsiImRm are not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) **[End CB015668-A]**, in TDD FR1 in CSI-IM slot, if a SI-Msg is scheduled in this CSI-IM slot, the starting PRB startRbSiMsg of the SI-Msg shall be modulo PRB\_GRANULARITY in order to keep the PDSCH sub areas (startPrb and size) multiples of PRB\_GRANULARITY (see 5G\_UP\_11022\_replaced([11350898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubpjFvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then gNB-DU shall increase of decrease the value of startRbSiMsg in this way.

If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, due to the scheduling of SI-Msg channel, gNB-DU shall split the current PDSCH sub area which contains the CORESET #0 in two PDSCH sub areas :

· one which contains the SI-msg starting with the startRbSiMsg **if mono BWP or dedicated BWP bottom aligned**and the PRBs which are above the SI-msg if mono BWP or dedicated BWP bottom aligned.\*\*\*\*

· one which contains the PRBs which are below the SI-msg if mono BWP dedicated BWP bottom aligned or above the SI-msg if dedicated BWPs top aligned.

The update and initialization of the PDSCH sub areas are described with more details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23452\_replaced([11175855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kumUKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and are done at to-be-scheduled list update step of the TD scheduler (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4327\_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.22.5.5.0-3 PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages Other parameters for the PDSCH SI-Msg transmissions (ID: 11166463)

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11166467`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Demodulated Reference Signal configuration parameters for the SI-Msg transmissions

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166473`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
The 5G-L2-PS sets the following  Demodulated Reference Signal configuration for the SI-Msg transmissions:

 The parameter “dmrsScramblingSequenceInt” is equal to the Physical Cell Identifier NIDD parameter “physCellId” under MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL object.

 The parameter “dlDmrsConfigType” is equal to 1.

 The parameter “dlDmrsLen” is equal to 1.

 The parameter “dlDmrsMappingType” is set according to the Time Domain Resource Allocation saved in the active context of SI-Msg and the associated SS/PBCH index (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3798\_replaced([11165937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjLTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The parameter “dlDmrsAddPos” is equal to 2.

 The parameter “dlDmrsTypeAPos” is equal to the NIDD parameter “dmrsTypeAPosition” under “MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL” object and received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq.

 The parameter “numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData” is equal to 2.

 The parameter “nscId” is equal to 0. This parameter is not used for the SI-Msg transmissions.

 The parameter “offsetRbDmrs” is set to 0.

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11166478`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Phase Tracking Reference Signal configuration

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11166484`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
The 5G-L2-PS does not activate the Phase Tracking Reference Signal (PT-RS) for the SI-Msg transmissions and uses the following setting:

 The parameter “dlPtrsFlag” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsTimeDensity” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsFrequencyDensity” is set to 0.

 The parameter “dlPtrsNumOfPorts” is set to 1.

 The parameter “dlPtrsResElemOffset” is set to 0.

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11166490`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Frequency and time domains configuration

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11166507`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
11166507:
PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
The 5G-L2-PS sets the frequency and time domains configuration for the SI-Msg transmisisons as follows:

 The parameter “startSymbol” is set to start symbol of the Time Domain Resource Allocation selected for the SI-Msg transmission and defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3825\_replaced([11166424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “numOfPdschSymbols” is set to length of the Time Domain Resource Allocation selected for the SI-Msg transmission and defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3825\_replaced([11166424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “startPrb” indicates the absolute position of the SI-Msg transmission and takes into account the position of the CORESET(0) within the whole bandwidth. The first MSB bit set to 1 ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "msbPos" in a blurry, light blue font against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11578.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]) in the coresetFreqDomain parameter of the CORESET(0) and the RB shift ([image-1][image\_desc]The image contains blurry text that reads "coresetFreqDomainRblShlfc".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11578.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]) are received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message. The starting PRB of the SI-Msg transmission(s) is computed in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3827\_replaced([11166434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[image-2][image\_desc]startPrb = 6 × (63 – msbPos) + coresetFreqDomainRbShift + startRbSimsg[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11578.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

 The parameter “numOfPrb” is set to number of RB compute for the SI-Msg and saved in the SI-Msg context as defined in the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3827\_replaced([11166434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) requirement.

 The parameter “rat0Bitmap” is set to 0x0000, as only the resource allocation type 1 is used for the SI-Msg transmissions.

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11166511`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Modulation and Coded Scheme

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11166518`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
The 5G-L2-PS applies the following Modulation and Coded Scheme setting:

 The parameter “mcs” as defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3802\_replaced([11166155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The parameter “mcsTable” is set to “max64QAM”.

 The parameter “modulationOrder” is set to QPSK (2).

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11166529`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
For the Layer to antenna port mapping configuration, the 5G-L2-PS applies the following setting:

 The parameter “numOfLayers” is set to 1.

 The parameter “antPort” is set to 0x8000.

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11166534`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Precoding antenna port to Radio Unit port settings

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11166542`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
The 5G-L2-PS applies the following setting for the precoding antenna port to Radio Unit port:

 The parameter “pdschBundleSize” is set to 4 (the UE assumes, without any impact, a bundle size set to 2).

 The precoding and spatial mode parameters are set according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3171\_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `11166548`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
Beamforming management parameters

---

**3.22.5.5.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11166552`)

PDSCH resource allocation of SI messages
For the eCPRI configuration, the following parameters are defined for beamforming management.

 numCeAxcIndex. The value corresponds to the number of Radio Unit Antenna ports available for the cell (2 or 4).

 ceAxcIndex. The Value corresponds to the indexes of Antenna-Carrier (AxC) containers selected for the PDCCH transmission in the cell between 0 to numCeAxcIndex-1.

 patternId. The value corresponds to the index of the pattern associated to the beam Index of the selected SS/PBCH for the transmission.

For CPRI configuration, the beamforming management is done by sending the DlData\_PatternConfigReq.

---

### 3.22.5.6 PDSCH payload management for the SI-Msg transmission

**3.22.5.6.0-1**  (ID: `11166567`)

PDSCH payload management for the SI-Msg transmission
11166567:
PDSCH payload management for the SI-Msg transmission
The 5G-L2-PS receives from the C-Plane in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message the ASN1 encoded SI-Msg in a Radio Link Control Transparent Mode (RLC-TM) Paquet Data Unit (PDU).

With the Transport Blocks Size defined during the LA process, the 5G-L2-PS builds a Medium Access Control (MAC) transparent PDU with the RCL-TM PDU and adds 0 padding bits if needed to reach the TBS.

Then, the 5G-L2-PS build the DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message, in order to send it with the DlData\_PdschSendReq to the L1, with the following parameters:

 The parameter “tbIndex” is set to 0.

 The parameter “tbFragmentOffset\_bits” is set to 0.

 The parameter “tbFragmentSize\_bytes” is computed from the Transport Block Size (TBS) defined during the link adaptation process defined in the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3803\_replaced([11166166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$tbFragmentSize\_{bytes} = \frac{TBS}{8}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11588.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

 The payload corresponding to the MAC PDU above.

---

### 3.22.5.7 DCI Format 1_0 content

**3.22.5.7.0-1**  (ID: `11166588`)

DCI Format 1\_0 content
11166588:
DCI Format 1\_0 content
The DCI Format 1\_0 for the SI-Msg transmissions is detailed hereafter.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DCI Format 1\_0 size for SI transmissions |  |  |  |
| Field description | Initial BWP size (RB) |  |  |
| 24 | 48 | 96 |  |
| Frequency Domain Resource Allocation | 9 | 11 | 13 |
| Time Domain Resource Allocation | 4 |  |  |
| VRB-to-PRB mapping | 1 |  |  |
| Modulation and coding scheme | 5 |  |  |
| Redundancy version | 2 |  |  |
| System information indicator | 1 |  |  |
| Reserved bits | 15 |  |  |
| Total (without 24 CRC bits) | 37 | 39 | 41 |
|  |  |  |  |
| The frequency domain resource allocation size is defined according to the position of the CORESET associated to the Type0A-PDCCH. The resource allocation type 1 is used. The Resource Indication Value (RIV) is computed with the following information: |  |  |  |
|  Number of RB for the SI-Msg transmission (nRbSiMsg). |  |  |  |
|  Number of RB for the CORESET(0) ([image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N RB CORESET(0)". The text is in a light blue color and appears to be slightly blurred. The "N" is large and in the foreground, with "RB" as a superscript above and to the right of the "N". Below the "N" and slightly to the right is the word "CORESET", and to the right of that is "(0)" in parentheses.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11590.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]). |  |  |  |
|  Index of the RB start (startRbSiMsg). |  |  |  |
| [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in LaTeX. The formula defines a piecewise function named `rivSiMsg`. |  |  |  |
| The function is defined as follows: |  |  |  |
| For the condition `(nRbSiMsg - 1) <= |N_CORESET(0)^RB / 2|`, the value of `rivSiMsg` is `N_CORESET(0)^RB * (nRbSiMsg - 1) + startRbSib1`. |  |  |  |
| For the condition `(nRbSiMsg - 1) > |N_CORESET(0)^RB / 2|`, the value of `rivSiMsg` is `N_CORESET(0)^RB * (N_CORESET(0)^RB - nRbSiMsg + 1) + (N_CORESET(0)^RB - 1 - startRbSiMsg)`. |  |  |  |
| The variables used in the formula are: |  |  |  |
| - `rivSiMsg` |  |  |  |
| - `N_CORESET(0)^RB` |  |  |  |
| - `nRbSiMsg` |  |  |  |
| - `startRbSib1`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11590.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] |  |  |  |
| The time domain resource allocation index for each SI-Msg transmission is the one defined by the 5G-L2-PS during the PDSCH time domain resource allocation of the SI-Msg. |  |  |  |
| VRB-to-PRB mapping is set to Non-Interleaved (0). |  |  |  |
| The Modulation and Coding Scheme field is set to the value of IMCS computed according to the transport block size and coding rate expected for the SI-Msg (see section “SI-Msg initial transmission and retransmission pattern”). |  |  |  |
| The Redundancy version is set according to the transmission index of the SI-Msg for a given SS/PBCH block configured (the first index is the initial transmission and the others the retransmissions) as follows. |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Transmission index | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | 6 | 7 | 8 |
| Redundancy Version index | 0 | 2 | 3 | 1 | 0 | 2 | 3 | 1 |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The System information indicator is set to 1 for the SI messages. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

---

### 3.22.5.8 SI-Msg scheduling procedure

**3.22.5.8.0-1**  (ID: `11166598`)

SI-Msg scheduling procedure
For each occurences of SFN and slot for SI-Msg transmission, the 5G-L2 PS sends 3 messages to the 5G-L1-DL:

 The DlData\_PdcchSendReq.

 The DlData\_PdschSendReq.

 The DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq.

The SI-Msg scheduling is done before any other PDCCH/PDSCH resource allocation.

The 3 messages to broadacst the SI-Msg are always sent to only one subcell.

---

### 3.22.5.9 SI messages error handling and successful configuration

#### 3.22.5.9.1 SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed

##### 3.22.5.9.1.0-1 SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed procedure (ID: 11166614)

**3.22.5.9.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12514709`)

SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
12514709:
SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
When the 5G-L2-PS receives the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq with a field “informationBlockType” set to “SystemInformationMessage”, the payload size of each SI messages is checked whatever the “systemInformationTargetRate” value with the MCS9 and the 3GPP maximum TBS for SI (2976 bits).
The 5G-L2-PS checks the payload size sent by the C-Plane according to the number of RB associated to the coreset(0), and the TDRA allowing PDSCH mapping type A with a SLIV using the start OFDM symbol defined by the front-loaded DM-RS Type A position and the largest length available which does not include the OFDM symbols for the CSI-RS transmissions (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3798\_replaced([11165937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjLTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
On the 5G-L2-PS side, the information received in PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq are not taken into account and the SIB1 passive context is not valid and could not become active, when the check, detailed hereafter, is failed.
The first step is to compute the intermediate TBS (*TBS*min) as follows.**[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines `TBSmin` in two parts.
The first part is:
`TBSmin = | (NRE × (nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging) × RMcs) / 2^(n+9) | × 2^n`
The second part, which is conditional on `n`, is:
`= max(3, | Log2( (NRE × nRbCch - minRbReservedForNonSiPaging × Rmcs) / 2^9 ) | - 6)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
With
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "nRbCch". The text is blurry and appears to be in a light blue color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:
Number of Resource Block available for the coreset(0) part (24, 48 or 96) according to the value of the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter.
 
 
| | | | | | | | | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Number of RB of the CORESET(0) bandwidth | | | | | | | | | | | |
| SS/PBCH SCS (kHz) | | 15 | | 30 | | 30 (n79[CB009173-B] and n104 [End CB009173-B]) | | 120 | | 240 | |
| Common SCS (kHz) | | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 15 | 30 | 60 | 120 | 60 | 120 |
| type0CoresetConfigurationIndex | 0 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 |
| 1 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 |
| 2 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 48 |
| 3 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 24 | 48 | 48 | 96 | 48 |

| 5 | 24 | 24 | 48 | 24 | 96 | 48 | 48 | 24 | - | 24 |

| 14 | 96 | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |
| 15 | - | - | - | 48 | - | - | - | - | - | - |
 
minRbReservedForNonSiPaging:
 Minimum *number of RBs reserved for other UEs RNTI that could be used to scheduled using DCI 1\_0 format. (NIDD Parameter /NRBTS/NRCELL/minRbReservedForNonSiPaging)*
*Note:* if NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is False, then minRbReservedForNonSiPaging parameter shall not be referred.**
*N*RE:\*\*
Number of Resource Elements (RE) available per PRB. It depends on the time domain allocations previously selected for the SI message transmissions.
The number of RE available per PRB is computed as follow, with the number of OFDM symbol of the time domain allocation [image-2][image\_desc](SLIV_length)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.004.png[/image\_path][/image-2] selected.
[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $N\_{RB} = 12 \times (SLIV\_{length} - nDmRsSymb)$. The equation is written in white text against a white background. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.005.png[/image\_path][/image-3]
The number of OFDM symbols booked for the additional and/or front loaded PDSCH DM-RS [image-4][image\_desc](n DmRsSymb)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.006.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is defined as follow according to the following table and formula.
 
[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation defining "duration". The equation is presented as a piecewise function.
The first case, when `dDmrsMappingType = TypeA`, defines `duration` as the sum of `SLIV_start` and `SLIV_length`.
The second case, when `dDmrsMappingType = TypeB`, defines `duration` as `SLIV_length`.
The equation is written as:
`duration = {
SLIV_start + SLIV_length if dDmrsMappingType = TypeA
SLIV_length if dDmrsMappingType = TypeB
}`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.007.png[/image\_path][/image-5]
The following table indicates the number of OFDM symbols handling the DM-RS according to the duration computed above.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Duration | Number of DM-RS OFDM symbols |
| <8 | 1 |
| 8 or 9 | 2 |
| 10 to 14 | 3 |
|  |  |
| [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains text that appears to be a string of characters. The text is blurry and difficult to read clearly. The characters visible are: "min PRBReservedFdmC.chSIPaging".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.008.png[/image\_path][/image-6]: |  |
| Minimum PRB reserved for other UEs RNTI using DCI 1\_0 |  |
| [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "R MCS" in a stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are blue and purple, with a slight blur. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11597.009.png[/image\_path][/image-7]: |  |
| Target coding rate is set to 679 (MCS9). |  |
| Then, the 5G-L2-PS gets the real TBS by selecting the closest TBS in the following list that is not less than the TBSmin computed previously and not greater than 2976 bits (maximum size of the Transport Block for a SI message). |  |

| 2 | 32 | 32 | 352 | 62 | 1320 | 92 | 3752 |
| 3 | 40 | 33 | 368 | 63 | 1352 | 93 | 3824 |
| 4 | 48 | 34 | 384 | 64 | 1416 |  |  |
| 5 | 56 | 35 | 408 | 65 | 1480 |  |  |
| 6 | 64 | 36 | 432 | 66 | 1544 |  |  |
| 7 | 72 | 37 | 456 | 67 | 1608 |  |  |
| 8 | 80 | 38 | 480 | 68 | 1672 |  |  |
| 9 | 88 | 39 | 504 | 69 | 1736 |  |  |
| 10 | 96 | 40 | 528 | 70 | 1800 |  |  |
| 11 | 104 | 41 | 552 | 71 | 1864 |  |  |
| 12 | 112 | 42 | 576 | 72 | 1928 |  |  |
| 13 | 120 | 43 | 608 | 73 | 2024 |  |  |
| 14 | 128 | 44 | 640 | 74 | 2088 |  |  |

| 23 | 208 | 53 | 984 | 83 | 2728 |  |  |

| 26 | 256 | 56 | 1128 | 86 | 2976 |  |  |
| 27 | 272 | 57 | 1160 | 87 | 3104 |  |  |
| 28 | 288 | 58 | 1192 | 88 | 3240 |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The 5G-L2-PS compare the TBS obtained to each SI message payload size sent by the C-Plane. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| If the payload size received does not fit the TBS, the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message is sent back to the C-Plane with the following content and the list of data associated to each SI message size check failed: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The status is set to “NOK”. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The cause is set to 0x00010000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the maximum TBS allowed for the SI messages (see above). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is equal to the SLIV of the time domain resource allocation used. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is equal to the frequency domain resource allocation (it could be 24 or 48 or 96 RBs). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the index of the first SI message with a failed size check. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is set to the payload size for the first SI message with a failed size check. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[5]” element is set to the index of the second SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[6]” element is set to the payload size for the second SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[7]” element is set to the index of the third SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[8]” element is set to the payload size for the third SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[9]” element is set to the index of the fourth SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[10]” element is set to the payload size for the fourth SI message with a failed size check, if it exists. Otherwise, the value is set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  The “diagnosticInformation[11-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

##### 3.22.5.9.1.0-2 SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed fault structure (ID: 11166704)

**3.22.5.9.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11166714`)

SI message payload size exceeding the Transport Block Size allowed
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00010000.

This cause indicates “Incorrect systemInformationTargetRate [CB009550-B] or "minRbReservedForNonSiPaging" [End CB009550-B] parameter setting for one or several SI messages”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are filled with the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]” reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message.

---

#### 3.22.5.9.2 SI message slot selection failure

##### 3.22.5.9.2.0-1 SI message slot selection failure procedure (ID: 11166745)

**3.22.5.9.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166748`)

SI message slot selection failure
The error is detected when for at least one SS/PBCH configured, there is no capability to transmit the associated SI message. In that case, the 5G-L2-PS stops the SI messages processing, set all passive context already updated to not valid, builds the bitmap of the SS/PBCH configured and the bitmap of the SS/PBCH without any SI message transmission capability. Then, the 5G-L2-PS sends back to the C-Plane the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following content:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00020000.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follows:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is the 32 MSB of the configured SS/PBCH bitmap.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is the 32 LSB of the configured SS/PBCH bitmap.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is the 32 MSB of the SS/PBCH bitmap without SI message transmission capability.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is the 32 LSB of the SS/PBCH bitmap without SI message transmission capability.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.22.5.9.2.0-2 SI message slot selection failure fault structure (ID: 11166754)

**3.22.5.9.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11166761`)

SI message slot selection failure
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00020000.

This cause indicates “One or several SS/PBCH have no grant capability for SI message transmission due to incorrect SI-Window size or Type0A-PDCCH or Paging or CSI-RS for tracking or frame structure configuration”

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are filled with the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]” reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message.

#### 3.22.5.9.3 Discrepancy between the SIB1 and the SI messages coverages

##### 3.22.5.9.3.0-1 Discrepancy between the SIB1 and the SI messages coverages procedure (ID: 11166782)

**3.22.5.9.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166787`)

Discrepancy between the SIB1 and the SI messages coverages
When the operator set the systemInformationTargetRate parameter to a value not equal to 1, then the 5G-L2-PS computes the Link Adaptation settings to match the expected target rate. Nevertheless, according to the SI message payload size, the size of the Control Resource Set used for the SI messages Downlink Control Information, the number of SS/PBCH configured, the SI window size and the slot used for other common channels and CSI-RS for tracking, it is possible that the expected target rate set by the operator is not the one obtained after several transmissions of SI messages.

When the systemInformationTargetRate parameter is set to 1, there is no discrepancy as the expected target rate and the one obtained is the same and is defined by the MCS used to handle the SI message payload sizes sent by the C-Plane.

The 5G-L2-PS selects, as the reference, the best estimated rate of the SIB1 (the lowest value) among all SS/PBCH configured.

Then the 5G-L2-PS compares it to the estimated rate computed for each SI message configured during the Link Adaptation process of SI messages.

When the delta between estimated rate of SI message and the best estimated rate of the SIB1 is greater than a threshold defined hereafter according to the MCS used for the SI message transmissions, the 5G-L2-PS saves the data for up to the three first SI messages with the discrepancy coverage and the bitmap of all SI messages with the issue in order to report them in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message. The 5G-L2-PS does not stop the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq processing for this discrepancy coverage detection. The threshold is set according to MCS computed for each SI message as follows.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Modulation and coding scheme | Threshold |
| 0 to 2 | 40 |
| 3 to 4 | 60 |
| 5 to 9 | 80 |

At the end of the processing, if there is no other error type detected, the 5G-L2-PS reports to the C-Plane, the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “OK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00030000.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is the concatenation of the value of the rate used as the reference in the check (2 most significant bytes) and the value of the threshold used when the MSC is between MCS0 and MCS2 (2 least significant bytes).

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is the concatenation of the value of the threshold used when the MSC is between MCS3 and MCS4 (2 most significant bytes) and the value of the threshold used when the MSC is between MCS5 and MCS9 (2 least significant bytes).

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is the bitmap of SI messages with the coverage discrepancy. The position within the bitmap is the SI message index.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]”.element is the concatenation of the index of the first SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its TBS (2 least significant bytes).

 The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is the concatenation of the SLIV associated to the first SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its MCS (2 least significant bytes).

 The “diagnosticInformation[5]” element is the concatenation of the number of RB associated to the first SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its number of transmissions (2 least significant bytes).

 The “diagnosticInformation[6]”.element is the concatenation of the index of the second SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its TBS (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[7]” element is the concatenation of the SLIV associated to the second SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its MCS (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[8]” element is the concatenation of the number of RB associated to the second SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its number of transmissions (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[9]”.element is the concatenation of the index of the third SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its TBS (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[10]” element is the concatenation of the SLIV associated to the third SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its MCS (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[11]” element is the concatenation of the number of RB associated to the third SI message with the coverage discrepancy (2 most significant bytes) and its number of transmissions (2 least significant bytes), if needed. Otherwise, it is set to 0x00000000.

 The “diagnosticInformation[12-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

#### 3.22.5.9.4 Default SI message processing error report

##### 3.22.5.9.4.0-1 Default SI message processing error report procedure (ID: 11166824)

**3.22.5.9.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166829`)

Default SI message processing error report
When the 5G-L2-PS detects any other error, it may or may not stop the processing according default defense procedure, but always reports the issue to the C-Plane through the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message the with the following information:

 The status is set to “OK” or “NOK”.

The expected status must be defined according to the expected behavior from the design point of view:

 If it is “OK”, then the configuration will be considered degraded by the C-Plane and a BTS fault will be raised to the fault services, but the cell will be degraded.

 If it is “NOK”, then the configuration will be considered as failed by the C-Plane and the cell will be not operational or degraded according to the cell context.

 The cause is set to 0x00040000.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array may be fulfilled with additional data defined by the design team.

---

##### 3.22.5.9.4.0-2 Default SI message processing error report fault structure (ID: 11166835)

**3.22.5.9.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11166840`)

The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00040000.

This cause indicates “Internal SI message processing error”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]”elements reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfo-ConfigurationResp message.

#### 3.22.5.9.5 Invalid SI message configuration with more than one Public Warning System SIB

##### 3.22.5.9.5.0-1 Invalid SI message configuration with more than one Public Warning System SIB fault structure (ID: 11166861)

**3.22.5.9.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166867`)

Invalid SI message configuration with more than one Public Warning System SIB
If one SI-Msg contains a "pwsType" with more than one bit set to "1", the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message is sent back to the C-Plane with the following content:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00050000.

This cause indicates "Invalid SI message configuration with more than one Public Warning System SIB".

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is set to the index of the SI message with more than one bit set to 1 in the "pwsType".

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is set to the "pwsType" value received from the C-Plane for this SI-Msg.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

#### 3.22.5.9.6 Invalid number of SI messages configured

##### 3.22.5.9.6.0-1 Invalid number of SI messages configured counting procedure (ID: 11166887)

**3.22.5.9.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11166908`)

Invalid number of SI messages configured
11166908:
Invalid number of SI messages configured
When the 5G-L2-PS receives the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq with a field “informationBlockType” set to “SystemInformationMessage”, the 5G-L2-PS checks the number of SI-Msgs configured for each combination of PWS configured with the SIB1 (through the parameter pwsType of SIB1).

The 5G-L2-PS counts the number of SI messages for each combination of PWS types by selecting first all SI-Msg(s) with pwsType set to 0 and add the SI-Msg(s) with the expected pwsType if the index of the SI-Msg is not already present in the list of all SI-Msg(s) with pwsType set to 0. Then the 5G-L2-PS, uses this number of SI-Msg expected and verifies it is lower or equal the maximum number of SI-Msg (nSiMsgmax) according to the SI configuration (SI-Window/SIB periodicity).

[image-0][image\_desc]$nSiMsg\_{max} = \lfloor \frac{|SiMsgPeriodicity\_{min} \times 10 \times 2^\mu|}{SiMsgWindow} \rfloor$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11633.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

With,

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "siMsgPeriodicity\_min" in a blurry, light blue font against a white background. The text is slightly pixelated and has a soft focus effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11633.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:

Minimum sibPeriodicity (radio frame) among all configured in the Cell

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "stMsgWindow" in a blurry, light gray font against a white background. The text is horizontally aligned.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11633.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]:

siWindowLength (slot) configured in the Cell

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, abstract shot of what appears to be a metallic surface with a gradient of colors. The dominant colors are shades of silver, blue, and a hint of peach or light brown. The surface has a reflective quality, with highlights and shadows creating a sense of depth and dimension. The lighting seems to be coming from the left, casting a soft glow on the metallic material. The overall impression is one of sleekness and modernity, possibly representing a part of a machine, a piece of art, or a design element. There is no discernible text or table in the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_11633.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]:

Numerology associated to the Sub Carrier Spacing of the channel bandwidth and defined at the NIDD level.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Numerology | SCSCommon (kHz) |
| 0 | 15 |
| 1 | 30 |
| 2 | 60 |
| 3 | 120 |

##### 3.22.5.9.6.0-2 Invalid number of SI messages configured check failure procedure (ID: 11166912)

**3.22.5.9.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11166918`)

Invalid number of SI messages configured
When the check is failed, then the 5G-L2-PS reports a negative acknowledgement in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK”.

 The cause is set to 0x00060000.

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the pwsType.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is equal to the number of SI-Msg count by the 5GL2-PS for this PWS type (all SI-Msg without pwsType and if it is not redundant SI-Msg index, the one with the expected PWS type).

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is equal to the maximum number of SI-Msg computed by the 5G-L2-PS.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the minimum SIB periodicity selected by the 5G-L2-PS.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is set to the SI window used.

 The “diagnosticInformation[5-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.22.5.9.6.0-3 Invalid number of SI messages configured faut structure (ID: 11166924)

**3.22.5.9.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11166929`)

Invalid number of SI messages configured
The C-plane will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId):  EFaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting.

 The fault state (faultState):   EFaultState\_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity):

 EFaultSeverity\_OutOfOrder.

This fault severity is used when the C-Plane is starting the cell configuration (the cell is not operational).

 EFaultSeverity\_Degraded.

This fault severity is used when the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationReq message is an online modification of the system information (the cell was already configured successfully before this modification).

 The object type (objectType):  EObjectType\_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId):  Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] defines the additional cause: 0x00060000.

This cause indicates “Incorrect number of SI-Messages configured”.

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are filled with the “diagnosticInformation[0-12]” reported by the 5G-L2-PS in the PsCell\_SystemInfoConfigurationResp message.

---

The additional text sent in the alarm by the gNB is detailed hereafter, when faultId is set to FaultId\_IncorrectCellParameterSetting with the extraFaultInfo[0] set to 0x00060000.

Cause: Invalid number of SI-Messages configured
